    Permissions=;
    DataCaptionFields=No.,Description;
    OnInsert=BEGIN
               IF "No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                 GetInvtSetup;
                 InvtSetup.TESTFIELD("Item Nos.");
                 NoSeriesMgt.InitSeries(InvtSetup."Item Nos.",xRec."No. Series",0D,"No.","No. Series");
               END;

               // Begin \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\
               //09.27.02 DRR - Added If statement for configured item
               IF NOT "Configured Item" THEN BEGIN
                 Commissionable := TRUE;
                 "Allow Invoice Disc." := TRUE;
                 //"Allow Item/Cust. Disc." := TRUE;  //MOD
               END;
               "Costing Method" := InvtSetup."Def. Costing Method";
               "Insert Date" := WORKDATE;
               "Insert Time" := TIME;
               "Insert User ID" := USERID;
               "RoHS Compliant" := TRUE;
               // End ////////////////////////////////
               DimMgt.UpdateDefaultDim(
                 DATABASE::Item,"No.",
                 "Global Dimension 1 Code","Global Dimension 2 Code");

               //Update Description and "Catalog Item" from OLD Items Data
               OldItemsDataG.RESET;
               IF OldItemsDataG.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
                 VALIDATE("Catalog Item",OldItemsDataG."Catalog Item");
                 CLEAR(CatalogItemG);
                 IF OldItemsDataG."Catalog Item" = TRUE THEN
                   CatalogItemG := 'TRUE'
                 ELSE
                   CatalogItemG := 'FALSE';
                  MESSAGE('Catalog Item field is updated as %1 from NAV 2009 Items data',CatalogItemG);
               END;

               //>>WI 09.17.18
               SalesReceivablesSetup.GET;
               IF SalesReceivablesSetup."Change Log for Website Items" THEN
                 CheckToSendtoWebsite(0,TRUE);
               //<<WI 09.17.18
             END;

    OnModify=BEGIN
               "Last Date Modified" := TODAY;

               PlanningAssignment.ItemChange(Rec,xRec);

               //>>WI 09.17.18
               SalesReceivablesSetup.GET;
               IF SalesReceivablesSetup."Change Log for Website Items" THEN
                 CheckToSendtoWebsite(1,TRUE);
               //<<WI 09.17.18
             END;

    OnDelete=VAR
               BinContent@1000 : Record 7302;
               ItemCrossReference@1001 : Record 5717;
               SocialListeningSearchTopic@1002 : Record 871;
               ItemSpecification@1000000001 : Record 50087;
               ItemSpecification2@1000000000 : Record 50088;
               UserSetup@1000000002 : Record 91;
               TaxonomyItem@1000000003 : Record 50183;
             BEGIN
               //HG
               UserSetup.GET(USERID);
               IF NOT UserSetup."Rename/Delete Items" THEN
                 ERROR(Text50000);
               //HG

               CheckJournalsAndWorksheets(0);
               CheckDocuments(0);

               MoveEntries.MoveItemEntries(Rec);

               ServiceItem.RESET;
               ServiceItem.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               IF ServiceItem.FIND('-') THEN
                 REPEAT
                   ServiceItem.VALIDATE("Item No.",'');
                   ServiceItem.MODIFY(TRUE);
                 UNTIL ServiceItem.NEXT = 0;

               ItemBudgetEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Analysis Area","Budget Name","Item No.");
               ItemBudgetEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemBudgetEntry.DELETEALL(TRUE);

               ItemSub.RESET;
               ItemSub.SETRANGE(Type,ItemSub.Type::Item);
               ItemSub.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
               ItemSub.DELETEALL;

               ItemSub.RESET;
               ItemSub.SETRANGE("Substitute Type",ItemSub."Substitute Type"::Item);
               ItemSub.SETRANGE("Substitute No.","No.");
               ItemSub.DELETEALL;

               SKU.RESET;
               SKU.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.");
               SKU.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               SKU.DELETEALL;

               NonstockItemMgt.NonstockItemDel(Rec);
               CommentLine.SETRANGE("Table Name",CommentLine."Table Name"::Item);
               CommentLine.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
               CommentLine.DELETEALL;

               ItemVend.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.");
               ItemVend.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemVend.DELETEALL;

               SalesPrice.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               SalesPrice.DELETEALL;

               SalesLineDisc.SETRANGE(Type,SalesLineDisc.Type::Item);
               SalesLineDisc.SETRANGE(Code,"No.");
               SalesLineDisc.DELETEALL;

               SalesPrepmtPct.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               SalesPrepmtPct.DELETEALL;

               PurchPrice.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               PurchPrice.DELETEALL;

               PurchLineDisc.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               PurchLineDisc.DELETEALL;

               PurchPrepmtPct.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               PurchPrepmtPct.DELETEALL;

               ItemTranslation.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemTranslation.DELETEALL;

               ItemUnitOfMeasure.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemUnitOfMeasure.DELETEALL;

               ItemVariant.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemVariant.DELETEALL;

               ExtTextHeader.SETRANGE("Table Name",ExtTextHeader."Table Name"::Item);
               ExtTextHeader.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
               ExtTextHeader.DELETEALL(TRUE);

               IF ItemAnalysisViewEntry.READPERMISSION THEN BEGIN    //ICS
                 ItemAnalysisViewEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
                 ItemAnalysisViewEntry.DELETEALL;
               END;

               ItemAnalysisBudgViewEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemAnalysisBudgViewEntry.DELETEALL;

               PlanningAssignment.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               PlanningAssignment.DELETEALL;

               BOMComp.RESET;
               BOMComp.SETRANGE("Parent Item No.","No.");
               BOMComp.DELETEALL;

               TroubleshSetup.RESET;
               TroubleshSetup.SETRANGE(Type,TroubleshSetup.Type::Item);
               TroubleshSetup.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
               TroubleshSetup.DELETEALL;

               ResSkillMgt.DeleteItemResSkills("No.");
               DimMgt.DeleteDefaultDim(DATABASE::Item,"No.");

               ItemIdent.RESET;
               ItemIdent.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.");
               ItemIdent.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemIdent.DELETEALL;

               ServiceItemComponent.RESET;
               ServiceItemComponent.SETRANGE(Type,ServiceItemComponent.Type::Item);
               ServiceItemComponent.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
               ServiceItemComponent.MODIFYALL("No.",'');

               BinContent.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.");
               BinContent.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               BinContent.DELETEALL;

               ItemCrossReference.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemCrossReference.DELETEALL;

               IF NOT SocialListeningSearchTopic.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                 SocialListeningSearchTopic.FindSearchTopic(SocialListeningSearchTopic."Source Type"::Item,"No.");
                 SocialListeningSearchTopic.DELETEALL;
               END;


               //Start ItemSpecification
               ItemSpecification.RESET;
               ItemSpecification.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemSpecification.DELETEALL;
               //Stop ItemSpecification

               //Start ItemSpecification
               ItemSpecification2.RESET;
               ItemSpecification2.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               ItemSpecification2.DELETEALL;
               //Stop ItemSpecification

               //Start IndustrialStandards
               IndustrialStandards.RESET;
               IndustrialStandards.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               IndustrialStandards.DELETEALL;
               //Stop IndustrialStandards

               //>>WI 09.17.18
               SalesReceivablesSetup.GET;
               IF SalesReceivablesSetup."Change Log for Website Items" THEN
                 CheckToSendtoWebsite(2,TRUE);
               //>>Taxonomy Items
               TaxonomyItem.RESET;
               TaxonomyItem.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
               TaxonomyItem.DELETEALL;
               //<<Taxonomy Items

               //<<WI 09.17.18
             END;

               IF "No." <> xRec."No." THEN BEGIN
                 IF TaxonomyItem.GET(xRec."No.") THEN
                   TaxonomyItem.RENAME("No.");
               END;
               //<<HGR 07.26.18 Taxonomy Item
             END;

    { 99000773;;Order Tracking Policy;Option      ;OnValidate=VAR
                                                                ReservEntry@1000 : Record 337;
                                                                ActionMessageEntry@1001 : Record 99000849;
                                                                TempReservationEntry@1002 : TEMPORARY Record 337;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                IF "Order Tracking Policy" <> "Order Tracking Policy"::None THEN
                                                                  TESTFIELD(Type,Type::Inventory);
                                                                IF xRec."Order Tracking Policy" = "Order Tracking Policy" THEN
                                                                  EXIT;
                                                                IF "Order Tracking Policy" > xRec."Order Tracking Policy" THEN BEGIN
                                                                  MESSAGE(Text99000000 +
                                                                    Text99000001,
                                                                    SELECTSTR("Order Tracking Policy",Text99000002));
                                                                END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                  ActionMessageEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Reservation Entry");
                                                                  ReservEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Variant Code","Location Code","Reservation Status");
                                                                  ReservEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
                                                                  ReservEntry.SETRANGE("Reservation Status",ReservEntry."Reservation Status"::Tracking,ReservEntry."Reservation Status"::Surplus);
                                                                  IF ReservEntry.FIND('-') THEN
                                                                    REPEAT
                                                                      ActionMessageEntry.SETRANGE("Reservation Entry",ReservEntry."Entry No.");
                                                                      ActionMessageEntry.DELETEALL;
                                                                      IF "Order Tracking Policy" = "Order Tracking Policy"::None THEN
                                                                        IF ReservEntry.TrackingExists THEN BEGIN
                                                                          TempReservationEntry := ReservEntry;
                                                                          TempReservationEntry."Reservation Status" := TempReservationEntry."Reservation Status"::Surplus;
                                                                          TempReservationEntry.INSERT;
                                                                        END ELSE
                                                                          ReservEntry.DELETE;
                                                                    UNTIL ReservEntry.NEXT = 0;

                                                                  IF TempReservationEntry.FIND('-') THEN
                                                                    REPEAT
                                                                      ReservEntry := TempReservationEntry;
                                                                      ReservEntry.MODIFY;
                                                                    UNTIL TempReservationEntry.NEXT = 0;
                                                                END;
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=[ENU=Order Tracking Policy;
                                                              ESM=Directiva seguim. ped.;
                                                              FRC=ChaŒnage dynamique;
                                                              ENC=Order Tracking Policy];
                                                   OptionCaptionML=[ENU=None,Tracking Only,Tracking & Action Msg.;
                                                                    ESM=Ninguna,Seguimiento,Seguim. y mens. acci¢n;
                                                                    FRC=&Aucun,Pistage seulement,Pistage & Message d'action;
                                                                    ENC=None,Tracking Only,Tracking & Action Msg.];
                                                   OptionString=None,Tracking Only,Tracking & Action Msg. }

    PROCEDURE AssistEdit@2() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      GetInvtSetup;
      InvtSetup.TESTFIELD("Item Nos.");
      IF NoSeriesMgt.SelectSeries(InvtSetup."Item Nos.",xRec."No. Series","No. Series") THEN BEGIN
        NoSeriesMgt.SetSeries("No.");
        EXIT(TRUE);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FindItemVend@5(VAR ItemVend@1000 : Record 99;LocationCode@1002 : Code[10]);
    VAR
      GetPlanningParameters@1004 : Codeunit 99000855;
    BEGIN
      TESTFIELD("No.");
      ItemVend.RESET;
      ItemVend.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      ItemVend.SETRANGE("Vendor No.",ItemVend."Vendor No.");
      ItemVend.SETRANGE("Variant Code",ItemVend."Variant Code");

      IF NOT ItemVend.FIND('+') THEN BEGIN
        ItemVend."Item No." := "No.";
        ItemVend."Vendor Item No." := '';
        GetPlanningParameters.AtSKU(SKU,"No.",ItemVend."Variant Code",LocationCode);
        IF ItemVend."Vendor No." = '' THEN
          ItemVend."Vendor No." := SKU."Vendor No.";
        IF ItemVend."Vendor Item No." = '' THEN
          ItemVend."Vendor Item No." := SKU."Vendor Item No.";
        ItemVend."Lead Time Calculation" := SKU."Lead Time Calculation";
      END;
      IF FORMAT(ItemVend."Lead Time Calculation") = '' THEN
        IF Vend.GET(ItemVend."Vendor No.") THEN
          ItemVend."Lead Time Calculation" := Vend."Lead Time Calculation";
      ItemVend.RESET;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ValidateShortcutDimCode@8(FieldNumber@1000 : Integer;VAR ShortcutDimCode@1001 : Code[20]);
    BEGIN
      DimMgt.ValidateDimValueCode(FieldNumber,ShortcutDimCode);
      DimMgt.SaveDefaultDim(DATABASE::Item,"No.",FieldNumber,ShortcutDimCode);
      MODIFY;
    END;

    PROCEDURE TestNoEntriesExist@1006(CurrentFieldName@1000 : Text[100]);
    VAR
      ItemLedgEntry@1001 : Record 32;
      PurchaseLine@1002 : Record 39;
    BEGIN
      IF "No." = '' THEN
        EXIT;

      ItemLedgEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.");
      ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      IF NOT ItemLedgEntry.ISEMPTY THEN
        ERROR(
          Text007,
          CurrentFieldName);

      PurchaseLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type",Type,"No.");
      PurchaseLine.SETFILTER(
        "Document Type",'%1|%2',
        PurchaseLine."Document Type"::Order,
        PurchaseLine."Document Type"::"Return Order");
      PurchaseLine.SETRANGE(Type,PurchaseLine.Type::Item);
      PurchaseLine.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
      IF PurchaseLine.FINDFIRST THEN
        ERROR(
          Text008,
          CurrentFieldName,
          PurchaseLine."Document Type");
    END;

    PROCEDURE TestNoOpenEntriesExist@4(CurrentFieldName@1000 : Text[100]);
    VAR
      ItemLedgEntry@1001 : Record 32;
    BEGIN
      ItemLedgEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.",Open);
      ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE(Open,TRUE);
      IF NOT ItemLedgEntry.ISEMPTY THEN
        ERROR(
          Text019,
          CurrentFieldName);
    END;

    PROCEDURE TestNoOpenDocumentsWithTrackingExist@42();
    VAR
      TrackingSpecification@1000 : Record 336;
      ReservationEntry@1001 : Record 337;
      RecRef@1004 : RecordRef;
      SourceType@1002 : Integer;
      SourceID@1003 : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      IF ItemTrackingCode2.Code = '' THEN
        EXIT;

      TrackingSpecification.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      IF TrackingSpecification.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        SourceType := TrackingSpecification."Source Type";
        SourceID := TrackingSpecification."Source ID";
      END ELSE BEGIN
        ReservationEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
        ReservationEntry.SETFILTER("Item Tracking",'<>%1',ReservationEntry."Item Tracking"::None);
        IF ReservationEntry.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
          SourceType := ReservationEntry."Source Type";
          SourceID := ReservationEntry."Source ID";
        END;
      END;

      IF SourceType = 0 THEN
        EXIT;

      RecRef.OPEN(SourceType);
      ERROR(OpenDocumentTrackingErr,RecRef.CAPTION,SourceID);
    END;

    PROCEDURE ItemSKUGet@11(VAR Item@1000 : Record 27;LocationCode@1001 : Code[10];VariantCode@1002 : Code[10]);
    VAR
      SKU@1003 : Record 5700;
    BEGIN
      IF Item.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
        IF SKU.GET(LocationCode,Item."No.",VariantCode) THEN
          Item."Shelf No." := SKU."Shelf No.";
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetInvtSetup@14();
    BEGIN
      IF NOT HasInvtSetup THEN BEGIN
        InvtSetup.GET;
        HasInvtSetup := TRUE;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE IsMfgItem@1() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT("Replenishment System" = "Replenishment System"::"Prod. Order");
    END;

    PROCEDURE IsAssemblyItem@24() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT("Replenishment System" = "Replenishment System"::Assembly);
    END;

    PROCEDURE HasBOM@18() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      CALCFIELDS("Assembly BOM");
      EXIT("Assembly BOM" OR ("Production BOM No." <> ''));
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetGLSetup@6();
    BEGIN
      IF NOT GLSetupRead THEN
        GLSetup.GET;
      GLSetupRead := TRUE;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ProdOrderExist@7() : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      ProdOrderLine.SETCURRENTKEY(Status,"Item No.");
      ProdOrderLine.SETFILTER(Status,'..%1',ProdOrderLine.Status::Released);
      ProdOrderLine.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      IF NOT ProdOrderLine.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);

      EXIT(FALSE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckSerialNoQty@15(ItemNo@1000 : Code[20];FieldName@1001 : Text[30];Quantity@1002 : Decimal);
    VAR
      ItemRec@1003 : Record 27;
      ItemTrackingCode3@1004 : Record 6502;
    BEGIN
      IF Quantity = ROUND(Quantity,1) THEN
        EXIT;
      IF NOT ItemRec.GET(ItemNo) THEN
        EXIT;
      IF ItemRec."Item Tracking Code" = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      IF NOT ItemTrackingCode3.GET(ItemRec."Item Tracking Code") THEN
        EXIT;
      IF ItemTrackingCode3."SN Specific Tracking" THEN
        ERROR(Text025,
          FieldName,
          TABLECAPTION,
          ItemNo,
          ItemTrackingCode3.FIELDCAPTION("SN Specific Tracking"));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckForProductionOutput@17(ItemNo@1000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      ItemLedgEntry@1001 : Record 32;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(ItemLedgEntry);
      ItemLedgEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Entry Type","Variant Code","Drop Shipment","Location Code","Posting Date");
      ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.",ItemNo);
      ItemLedgEntry.SETRANGE("Entry Type",ItemLedgEntry."Entry Type"::Output);
      IF NOT ItemLedgEntry.ISEMPTY THEN
        ERROR(Text026,FIELDCAPTION("Inventory Value Zero"),TABLECAPTION);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckBlockedByApplWorksheet@19();
    VAR
      ApplicationWorksheet@1000 : Page 521;
    BEGIN
      IF "Application Wksh. User ID" <> '' THEN
        ERROR(Text028,"No.",ApplicationWorksheet.CAPTION,"Application Wksh. User ID");
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowTimelineFromItem@20(VAR Item@1000 : Record 27);
    VAR
      ItemAvailTimeline@1001 : Page 5540;
    BEGIN
      ItemAvailTimeline.SetItem(Item);
      ItemAvailTimeline.RUN;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowTimelineFromSKU@21(ItemNo@1000 : Code[20];LocationCode@1001 : Code[10];VariantCode@1002 : Code[10]);
    VAR
      Item@1003 : Record 27;
    BEGIN
      Item.GET(ItemNo);
      Item.SETRANGE("No.",Item."No.");
      Item.SETRANGE("Variant Filter",VariantCode);
      Item.SETRANGE("Location Filter",LocationCode);
      ShowTimelineFromItem(Item);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckJournalsAndWorksheets@22(CurrFieldNo@1001 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      CheckItemJnlLine(CurrFieldNo);
      CheckStdCostWksh(CurrFieldNo);
      CheckReqLine(CurrFieldNo);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckItemJnlLine@44(CurrFieldNo@1000 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      ItemJnlLine.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
      IF NOT ItemJnlLine.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
        IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
          ERROR(Text023,TABLECAPTION,"No.",ItemJnlLine.TABLECAPTION);
        IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Type) THEN
          ERROR(CannotChangeFieldErr,FIELDCAPTION(Type),TABLECAPTION,"No.",ItemJnlLine.TABLECAPTION);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckStdCostWksh@45(CurrFieldNo@1000 : Integer);
    VAR
      StdCostWksh@1001 : Record 5841;
    BEGIN
      StdCostWksh.RESET;
      StdCostWksh.SETRANGE(Type,StdCostWksh.Type::Item);
      StdCostWksh.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
      IF NOT StdCostWksh.ISEMPTY THEN
        IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
          ERROR(Text023,TABLECAPTION,"No.",StdCostWksh.TABLECAPTION);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckReqLine@46(CurrFieldNo@1000 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      RequisitionLine.SETCURRENTKEY(Type,"No.");
      RequisitionLine.SETRANGE(Type,RequisitionLine.Type::Item);
      RequisitionLine.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
      IF NOT RequisitionLine.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
        IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
          ERROR(Text023,TABLECAPTION,"No.",RequisitionLine.TABLECAPTION);
        IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Type) THEN
          ERROR(CannotChangeFieldErr,FIELDCAPTION(Type),TABLECAPTION,"No.",RequisitionLine.TABLECAPTION);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckProdBOMLine@30(CurrFieldNo@1000 : Integer);
    VAR
      ProductionBOMVersion@1001 : Record 99000779;
    BEGIN
      ProdBOMLine.RESET;
      ProdBOMLine.SETCURRENTKEY(Type,"No.");
      ProdBOMLine.SETRANGE(Type,ProdBOMLine.Type::Item);
      ProdBOMLine.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
      IF ProdBOMLine.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
        IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO(Type) THEN
          ERROR(CannotChangeFieldErr,FIELDCAPTION(Type),TABLECAPTION,"No.",ProdBOMLine.TABLECAPTION);
        IF CurrFieldNo = 0 THEN
          REPEAT
            IF ProdBOMHeader.GET(ProdBOMLine."Production BOM No.") AND
               (ProdBOMHeader.Status = ProdBOMHeader.Status::Certified)
            THEN
              ERROR(Text004,TABLECAPTION,"No.");
            IF ProductionBOMVersion.GET(ProdBOMLine."Production BOM No.",ProdBOMLine."Version Code") AND
               (ProductionBOMVersion.Status = ProductionBOMVersion.Status::Certified)
            THEN
              ERROR(CannotDeleteItemIfProdBOMVersionExistsErr,TABLECAPTION,"No.");
          UNTIL ProdBOMLine.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE PreventNegativeInventory@33() : Boolean;
    VAR
      InventorySetup@1000 : Record 313;
    BEGIN
      CASE "Prevent Negative Inventory" OF
        "Prevent Negative Inventory"::Yes:
          EXIT(TRUE);
        "Prevent Negative Inventory"::No:
          EXIT(FALSE);
        "Prevent Negative Inventory"::Default:
          BEGIN
            InventorySetup.GET;
            EXIT(InventorySetup."Prevent Negative Inventory");
          END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcVAT@40() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF "Price Includes VAT" THEN BEGIN
        VATPostingSetup.GET("VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)","VAT Prod. Posting Group");
        CASE VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type" OF
          VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
            VATPostingSetup."VAT %" := 0;
          VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type"::"Sales Tax":
            ERROR(
              Text006,
              VATPostingSetup.FIELDCAPTION("VAT Calculation Type"),
              VATPostingSetup."VAT Calculation Type");
        END;
      END ELSE
        CLEAR(VATPostingSetup);

      EXIT(VATPostingSetup."VAT %" / 100);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcUnitPriceExclVAT@41() : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      GetGLSetup;
      IF 1 + CalcVAT = 0 THEN
        EXIT(0);
      EXIT(ROUND("Unit Price" / (1 + CalcVAT),GLSetup."Unit-Amount Rounding Precision"));
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcPurchReturn@12() : Decimal;
    VAR
      PurchLine@1000 : Record 39;
    BEGIN
      PurchLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type",Type,"No.","Variant Code","Drop Shipment","Location Code","Expected Receipt Date");
      PurchLine.SETRANGE("Document Type",PurchLine."Document Type"::"Return Order");
      PurchLine.SETRANGE(Type,PurchLine.Type::Item);
      PurchLine.SETRANGE("No.","No.");
      PurchLine.SETFILTER("Location Code",GETFILTER("Location Filter"));
      PurchLine.SETFILTER("Drop Shipment",GETFILTER("Drop Shipment Filter"));
      PurchLine.SETFILTER("Variant Code",GETFILTER("Variant Filter"));
      PurchLine.SETRANGE("Expected Receipt Date",GETRANGEMIN("Date Filter"),GETRANGEMAX("Date Filter"));
      PurchLine.CALCSUMS("Outstanding Qty. (Base)");
      EXIT(PurchLine."Outstanding Qty. (Base)");
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateUCCNo@1000000003();
    VAR
      NoSeriesLine@1000000000 : Record 309;
      NextNo@1000000001 : Code[20];
      UCCNo@1000000002 : Text[30];
      OldItemUPCNoL@1000000003 : Code[20];
    BEGIN
      //Update UCC No. From OLD Items Data
      CLEAR(OldItemUPCNoL);
      OldItemsDataG.RESET;
      IF OldItemsDataG.GET("No.") THEN BEGIN
        IF OldItemsDataG."Item UPC/EAN Number" <> '' THEN BEGIN
          OldItemUPCNoL := OldItemsDataG."Item UPC/EAN Number";
        END;
      END;

      IF OldItemUPCNoL <> '' THEN BEGIN
        UCCNo := OldItemUPCNoL;
        MESSAGE('Item UPC/EAN Number is updated as %1 from NAV 2009 Items data',UCCNo);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        //Get the next No. in the Series
        NoSeriesLine.GET('UCC',10000);
        IF NoSeriesLine."Last No. Used" = '' THEN BEGIN
          NextNo :=  NoSeriesLine."Starting No.";
        END ELSE BEGIN
          NextNo := INCSTR(NoSeriesLine."Last No. Used");
        END;

        //Write the last no used to No.Series Line Table
        NoSeriesLine."Last No. Used" := NextNo;
        NoSeriesLine.MODIFY;


        //Write Item UPC / EAN No. to Item
        UCCNo := NextNo;
      END;

      "Item UPC/EAN Number" := UCCNo;
      CreateUCCFontNo;
      MODIFY;
      //MESSAGE('The UCC No. for Item No. %1 is %2.',"No.","Item UPC/EAN Number");
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateUCCFontNo@1000000001();
    VAR
      UCCNo@1000000000 : Text[30];
      UCCFont@1000000001 : Text[30];
      OddNo@1000000002 : Integer;
      EvenNo@1000000003 : Integer;
      EvenStr1@1000000004 : Text[30];
      EvenStr2@1000000005 : Text[30];
      EvenStr3@1000000006 : Text[30];
      EvenStr4@1000000007 : Text[30];
      EvenStr5@1000000008 : Text[30];
      EvenNo1@1000000009 : Integer;
      EvenNo2@1000000010 : Integer;
      EvenNo3@1000000011 : Integer;
      EvenNo4@1000000012 : Integer;
      EvenNo5@1000000013 : Integer;
      OddStr1@1000000014 : Text[30];
      OddStr2@1000000015 : Text[30];
      OddStr3@1000000016 : Text[30];
      OddStr4@1000000017 : Text[30];
      OddStr5@1000000018 : Text[30];
      OddStr6@1000000019 : Text[30];
      OddNo1@1000000020 : Integer;
      OddNo2@1000000021 : Integer;
      OddNo3@1000000022 : Integer;
      OddNo4@1000000023 : Integer;
      OddNo5@1000000024 : Integer;
      OddNo6@1000000025 : Integer;
      CheckDigit@1000000026 : Integer;
      Precision@1000000027 : Integer;
      WorkChar@1000000028 : Text[1];
      i@1000000029 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      UCCNo := "Item UPC/EAN Number";

      // Get Sum of Odd No.'s
      OddStr1 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,1,1);
      OddStr2 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,3,1);
      OddStr3 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,5,1);
      OddStr4 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,7,1);
      OddStr5 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,9,1);
      OddStr6 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,11,1);
      EVALUATE(OddNo1,OddStr1);
      EVALUATE(OddNo2,OddStr2);
      EVALUATE(OddNo3,OddStr3);
      EVALUATE(OddNo4,OddStr4);
      EVALUATE(OddNo5,OddStr5);
      EVALUATE(OddNo6,OddStr6);
      OddNo := OddNo1 + OddNo2 + OddNo3 + OddNo4 + OddNo5 + OddNo6;
      OddNo := OddNo * 3;

      // Get Sum of Even No.'s
      EvenStr1 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,2,1);
      EvenStr2 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,4,1);
      EvenStr3 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,6,1);
      EvenStr4 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,8,1);
      EvenStr5 := COPYSTR(UCCNo,10,1);
      EVALUATE(EvenNo1,EvenStr1);
      EVALUATE(EvenNo2,EvenStr2);
      EVALUATE(EvenNo3,EvenStr3);
      EVALUATE(EvenNo4,EvenStr4);
      EVALUATE(EvenNo5,EvenStr5);
      EvenNo := EvenNo1 + EvenNo2 + EvenNo3 + EvenNo4 + EvenNo5;

      //CalculateCheck Digit
      //Precision := 10;
      //CheckDigit := (ROUND(OddNo + EvenNo,Precision,'>')) - (OddNo + EvenNo);
      //IF CheckDigit = 10 THEN
      //  CheckDigit := 0;
      CheckDigit := -1;
      REPEAT
        CheckDigit += 1;
      UNTIL (((OddNo + EvenNo + CheckDigit) MOD 10) = 0);

      //Add Checkdigit to end of UCC No.
      UCCNo := UCCNo + FORMAT(CheckDigit);

      "Item UPC with Check Digit" := UCCNo;
      // Create the Left Guard character
      WorkChar := COPYSTR(UCCNo,1,1);
      CASE WorkChar OF
        '0': WorkChar := 'D';
        '1': WorkChar := 'E';
        '2': WorkChar := 'F';
        '3': WorkChar := 'G';
        '4': WorkChar := 'H';
        '5': WorkChar := 'I';
        '6': WorkChar := 'J';
        '7': WorkChar := 'K';
        '8': WorkChar := 'L';
        '9': WorkChar := 'M';
      END;
      UCCFont := WorkChar + COPYSTR(UCCNo,2,5) + '.';

      // Translate the right side of the UPC
      FOR i := 7 TO 11 DO BEGIN
        WorkChar := COPYSTR(UCCNo,i,1);
        CASE WorkChar OF
          '0': WorkChar := 'a';
          '1': WorkChar := 'b';
          '2': WorkChar := 'c';
          '3': WorkChar := 'd';
          '4': WorkChar := 'e';
          '5': WorkChar := 'f';
          '6': WorkChar := 'g';
          '7': WorkChar := 'h';
          '8': WorkChar := 'i';
          '9': WorkChar := 'j';
        END;
        UCCFont := UCCFont + WorkChar;
      END;

      // Create the Right Guard character
      WorkChar := COPYSTR(UCCNo,STRLEN(UCCNo),1);
      CASE WorkChar OF
        '0': WorkChar := 'm';
        '1': WorkChar := 'n';
        '2': WorkChar := 'o';
        '3': WorkChar := 'p';
        '4': WorkChar := 'q';
        '5': WorkChar := 'r';
        '6': WorkChar := 's';
        '7': WorkChar := 't';
        '8': WorkChar := 'u';
        '9': WorkChar := 'v';
      END;
      UCCFont := UCCFont + WorkChar;

      "UPC Font Code" := UCCFont;
    END;

    PROCEDURE RemoveUCCNo@1000000002();
    BEGIN
      IF CONFIRM('Are you sure you want to remove the UPC Code from this item?',FALSE) THEN BEGIN
        "Item UPC/EAN Number" := '';
        "Item UPC with Check Digit" := '';
        MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE FilterItemNo@1000000000(ItemNoIn@1000000000 : Code[20]) ItemNoOut : Code[20];
    VAR
      i@1000000001 : Integer;
      TotalChar@1000000002 : Integer;
      TestChar@1000000003 : Code[1];
      DelChar@1000000004 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // ICS DFP 09.04.01 \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\
      // Remove characters that won't work in a file name
      ItemNoOut := ItemNoIn;
      TotalChar := STRLEN(ItemNoOut);
      i := 1;
      DelChar := FALSE;

      REPEAT
        TestChar := COPYSTR(ItemNoOut,i,1);
        IF TestChar = '*' THEN DelChar := TRUE;
        IF TestChar = '/' THEN DelChar := TRUE;
        IF TestChar = '\' THEN DelChar := TRUE;
        IF TestChar = '"' THEN DelChar := TRUE;
        IF TestChar = '''' THEN DelChar := TRUE;
      //02.28.03 DRR - Added this function\\\\\\\\\
        IF TestChar = '-' THEN DelChar := TRUE;
        IF TestChar = '_' THEN DelChar := TRUE;
        IF TestChar = '.' THEN DelChar := TRUE;
      //END/////////////////////////////////////////
        IF DelChar THEN
          BEGIN
            TotalChar -= 1;
            ItemNoOut := COPYSTR(ItemNoOut,1,(i-1)) + COPYSTR(ItemNoOut,(i+1));
            DelChar := FALSE;
          END
        ELSE
          i += 1;
      UNTIL i > TotalChar;
      // End /////////////////////////////////////////////
    END;

    PROCEDURE ShowPicture@1000000006();

    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateTechSheetDoc@1000000007(newFileP@1000000004 : Text[250]);
    VAR
      ItemSpec@1000000014 : Record 50087;
      wdApp@1000000003 : Automation "{00020905-0000-0000-C000-000000000046} 8.6:{000209FF-0000-0000-C000-000000000046}:Unknown Automation Server.Application";
      wdDoc@1000000002 : Automation "{00020905-0000-0000-C000-000000000046} 8.6:{00020906-0000-0000-C000-000000000046}:Unknown Automation Server.Document";
      wdRange@1000000001 : Automation "{00020905-0000-0000-C000-000000000046} 8.6:{0002095E-0000-0000-C000-000000000046}:Unknown Automation Server.Range";
      TemppathG@1000000000 : Text[250];
      WdVersionL@1000000005 : Text[30];
      LinkToFile@1000000007 : Variant;
      SaveWithDocument@1000000008 : Variant;
      Text50001@1000000013 : TextConst 'ENU=File Not Found In The Given Path.';
      FileName@1000000006 : Text[250];
      InvSetupL@1000000009 : Record 313;
    BEGIN
      //<<=====================02.01.2016=============================>>
      InvSetupL.GET;
      IF CREATE(wdApp,FALSE,TRUE) THEN BEGIN
        //TemppathG :=newFileP;
        TemppathG := InvSetupL."Tech. Data Sheet File Path";
        IF ItemSpec.GET("No.") THEN;
        IF NOT EXISTS(TemppathG) THEN
          ERROR(Text50001);

        wdDoc := wdApp.Documents.Add(TemppathG);
        wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Update;

        wdApp.Selection.ParagraphFormat.Alignment := 1;
        LinkToFile := FALSE;
        SaveWithDocument := TRUE;
        FileName := ItemSpec."Image URL";
        IF FileName <> '' THEN
          wdDoc.InlineShapes.AddPicture(FileName,LinkToFile, SaveWithDocument);

        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(1).Result;
        wdRange.Text := ItemSpec."Item No.";
        wdRange.Bold := 1;
        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(2).Result;
        wdRange.Text := Description;
        wdRange.Bold := 1;
        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(3).Result;
        wdRange.Text := ItemSpec."Technical 1";
        wdRange.Bold := 0;
        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(4).Result;
        wdRange.Text := ItemSpec."Technical 2";
        wdRange.Bold := 0;
        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(5).Result;
        wdRange.Text := ItemSpec."Technical 3";
        wdRange.Bold := 0;
        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(6).Result;
        wdRange.Text := ItemSpec."Technical 4";
        wdRange.Bold := 0;
        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(7).Result;
        wdRange.Text := ItemSpec."Technical 5";
        wdRange.Bold := 0;
        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(8).Result;
        wdRange.Text := ItemSpec."Technical 6";
        wdRange.Bold := 0;
        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(9).Result;
        wdRange.Text := ItemSpec."Technical 7";
        wdRange.Bold := 0;
        wdRange := wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Item(10).Result;
        wdRange.Text := ItemSpec."Technical 8";
        wdRange.Bold := 0;

        wdApp.Visible := TRUE;
        wdApp.ActiveDocument.Fields.Unlink;

        {
        WdVersionL := wdApp.Version;
        IF WdVersionL = '12.0' THEN
          wdDoc.SaveAs(FilePathForSave)
        ELSE
          wdDoc.SaveAs2(FilePathForSave);

        wdApp.Quit;
        }
      END;
      //<<=====================END=============================>>
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateItemPrices@1000000005();
    VAR
      PriceGroup@1000000000 : Record 6;
    BEGIN
      //07.24.02 DRR - Added to run report to fill in the Item Price Table when Unit Price changes///////////
      WITH SalesPrice2 DO BEGIN
        PriceGroup.RESET;
        IF PriceGroup.FINDFIRST THEN
          REPEAT
            INIT;
            "Item No." := Rec."No.";
            SalesPrice2."Sales Type" := SalesPrice2."Sales Type"::"Customer Price Group";
            SalesPrice2."Sales Code" := PriceGroup.Code;
            //"Unit of Measure Code" := 'EACH';
            "Unit of Measure Code" := "Base Unit of Measure";
            "Unit Price" := Rec."Unit Price";
            //"Allow Quantity Disc." := TRUE;
            //"Allow Cust./Item Disc." := TRUE;
            SalesPrice2."Allow Line Disc." := TRUE;
            "Allow Invoice Disc." := TRUE;
            IF NOT INSERT THEN
              MODIFY;
          UNTIL PriceGroup.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // END\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckItemStatus@1000000004();
    VAR
      Item@1000000000 : Record 27;
    BEGIN
      // ICS DFP 11.07.02 \\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\\
        IF "Item Status" < "Item Status"::Final THEN
          IF GUIALLOWED THEN BEGIN
            IF NOT CONFIRM(Text50002,FALSE) THEN
              ERROR('Item Status of Item %1 is not Final.' +
                    '\\Only Final Items can be Ordered.',
                    "No.");
          END ELSE
            ERROR('Item Status of Item %1 is not Final.' +
                '\\Only Final Items can be Ordered.',
                "No.");

      // End /////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateDimensionValue@1000000008(VAR Item@1000000000 : Record 27);
    VAR
      DimensionValue@1000000001 : Record 349;
      ItemCategory@1000000003 : Record 5722;
    BEGIN
      IF NOT DimensionValue.GET('PRODSUBTYPE',Item."Item Category Code") THEN BEGIN //Dimension Value for PRODSUBTYPE
        IF ItemCategory.GET(Item."Item Category Code") THEN BEGIN
          DimensionValue.INIT;
          DimensionValue.VALIDATE("Dimension Code",'PRODSUBTYPE');
          DimensionValue.VALIDATE(Code,ItemCategory.Code);
          DimensionValue.VALIDATE(Name,ItemCategory.Description);
          DimensionValue.INSERT(TRUE);
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateDefaultDimension@1000000018(VAR Item@1000000011 : Record 27);
    VAR
      DefaultDimension@1000000001 : Record 352;
      Dimension@1000000005 : Record 348;
    BEGIN
      IF Item."Item Category Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN// Dimension for PRODSUBTYPE
        IF NOT DefaultDimension.GET(27,Item."No.",'PRODSUBTYPE')THEN BEGIN
          DefaultDimension.INIT;
          DefaultDimension.VALIDATE("Table ID",27);
          DefaultDimension.VALIDATE("No.",Item."No.");
          DefaultDimension.VALIDATE("Dimension Code",'PRODSUBTYPE');
          DefaultDimension.VALIDATE("Dimension Value Code",Item."Item Category Code");
          DefaultDimension.INSERT(TRUE);
        END ELSE BEGIN
          DefaultDimension.VALIDATE("Dimension Value Code",Item."Item Category Code");
          DefaultDimension.MODIFY(TRUE);
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF DefaultDimension.GET(27,Item."No.",'PRODSUBTYPE')THEN
          DefaultDimension.DELETE;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE PopulateDimensionValue@1000000010(VAR ItemL@1000000000 : Record 27);

          DimensionValue.VALIDATE(Name,ItemL."Product Group");

      IF ItemL."Product Type" <> '' THEN BEGIN
        IF NOT DimensionValue.GET('PRODTYPE',ItemL."Product Type") THEN BEGIN //Dimension Value for PRODTYPE

          DimensionValue.VALIDATE(Name,ItemL."Product Type");

      IF ItemL."Product Sub Type 1" <> '' THEN BEGIN

          DimensionValue.INIT;
          DimensionValue.VALIDATE("Dimension Code",'PRODSUBTYPE1');
          DimensionValue.VALIDATE(Code,ItemL."Product Sub Type 1");
          DimensionValue.VALIDATE(Name,ItemL."Product Sub Type 1");
          DimensionValue.INSERT(TRUE);
        END;
      END;
      IF ItemL."Product Sub Type 2" <> '' THEN BEGIN

          DimensionValue.INIT;
          DimensionValue.VALIDATE("Dimension Code",'PRODSUBTYPE2');
          DimensionValue.VALIDATE(Code,ItemL."Product Sub Type 2");
          DimensionValue.VALIDATE(Name,ItemL."Product Sub Type 2");
          DimensionValue.INSERT(TRUE);
        END;
      END;
      IF ItemL."Product Sub Type 3" <> '' THEN BEGIN

          DimensionValue.INIT;

      END;
      IF ItemL.CostcenterDim <>'' THEN BEGIN

          DimensionValue.VALIDATE(Name,ItemL.CostcenterDim);

        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE PopulateDefaultDimension@1000000009(VAR ItemL@1000000011 : Record 27);

    PROCEDURE CheckToSendtoWebsite@1000000011(TypeP@1000000000 : 'Create,Update,Delete';ExternalP@1000000002 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SendItems@1000000001 : Record 50104;
      ItemCatalogEntry@1000000003 : Record 50081;
    BEGIN
      //>>WI 09.17.18
      IF TypeP <> 2 THEN BEGIN
        IF ("Base Unit of Measure" <> xRec."Base Unit of Measure") OR
          (Description <> xRec.Description) OR
          ("Description 2" <> xRec."Description 2") OR
          ("Mold Handle" <> xRec."Mold Handle") OR
          ("Weld Metal Code" <> xRec."Weld Metal Code") OR
          ("Box Qty." <> xRec."Box Qty.") OR
          ("Gen. Prod. Posting Group" <> xRec."Gen. Prod. Posting Group") OR
          ("Net Weight" <> xRec."Net Weight") OR
          ("Item UPC/EAN Number" <> xRec."Item UPC/EAN Number") OR
          ("Sleeve Req" <> xRec."Sleeve Req") OR
          (Width <> xRec.Width) OR
          (Length <> xRec.Length) OR
          (Thickness <> xRec.Thickness) OR
          ("UL Listing Code" <> xRec."UL Listing Code") OR
          (Run <> xRec.Run) OR
          (Tap <> xRec.Tap) OR
          ("Mold Family" <> xRec."Mold Family") OR
          ("Patent Status" <> xRec."Patent Status") OR
          ("Lead Time Calculation" <> xRec."Lead Time Calculation") OR
          ("Product Group" <> xRec."Product Group") OR
          ("Product Type" <> xRec."Product Type") OR
          ("Product Sub Type 1" <> xRec."Product Sub Type 1") OR
          ("Product Sub Type 2" <> xRec."Product Sub Type 2") OR
          ("Product Sub Type 3" <> xRec."Product Sub Type 3") OR
          ("Catalog Item" <> xRec."Catalog Item") OR
          (ExternalP) THEN BEGIN
            ItemCatalogEntry.RESET;
            ItemCatalogEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Catalog Code");
            ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
            ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Catalog Code",'WEBSITE');
            IF NOT ItemCatalogEntry.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
              SendItems.RESET;
              SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
              SendItems.SETRANGE(Type,TypeP);
              SendItems.SETRANGE("Process Status",SendItems."Process Status"::" ");
              IF SendItems.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                SendItems.RESET;
                SendItems.INIT;
                SendItems."Entry No." := 0;
                SendItems."Item No." := "No.";
                SendItems."Inserted By" := USERID;
                SendItems."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
                IF ExternalP AND (SkuID <> '') THEN
                  SendItems.Type := SendItems.Type::Update
                ELSE
                  SendItems.Type := TypeP;
                SendItems."Product Type" := SendItems."Product Type"::Product;
                SendItems.INSERT(TRUE);
              END;
            END;
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        SendItems.RESET;
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
        SendItems.SETFILTER(Type,'<>%1',TypeP);
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Process Status",SendItems."Process Status"::" ");
        IF NOT SendItems.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
          SendItems.DELETEALL;
        END;
        IF SkuID <> '' THEN BEGIN
          ItemCatalogEntry.RESET;
          ItemCatalogEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Catalog Code");
          ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","No.");
          ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Catalog Code",'WEBSITE');
          IF NOT ItemCatalogEntry.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            SendItems.RESET;
            SendItems.INIT;
            SendItems."Entry No." := 0;
            SendItems."Item No." := "No.";
            SendItems."Inserted By" := USERID;
            SendItems."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
            SendItems.Type := TypeP;
            SendItems.INSERT(TRUE);
          END;
        END;
      END;
      //<<WI 09.17.18
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      08.12.09 AU  - Added Frieght Terms Category Code
      11.22.04 RAS ICS3.03 - Added new field "Source Code Filter"
                           - Limit calculation of "Neg. Qty Adj" by new field
      ISS 01.07.04 DRR - Added Remove UCC Function
      //DELETED 04-06-06 !!08.28.02 DRR - Added to Calculate Std Cost for Configured Item No. MAT
      08.15.02 DRR - Added Non-Stock Item Field for Purchasing
      08.05.02 DRR - Remmed out code in UpdateSalesLines - dont remember why - I had a good reason though...
                     I think I did it so that we could update the Std cost field on the item card if there was
                     an item on a sales line
      07.24.02 DRR - Added to run report to fill in the Item Price Table when Unit Price changes
      09.21.01 DFP - Added "Mfg. Usage (Qty.)" flowfield
      08.09.01 DFP - Changed name of "Qty. on Hand - Grayslake"
                   - Added "Catalog Item" boolean (doesn't do anything yet)
      07.25.01 DFP - Added 50030-50032 Reorder fields
      07.13.01 DFP - Added field "Sort Dollars", "Running Total", key
      07.12.01 DFP - Added ABC Code
      07.03.01 DFP - Added 50003 Allow Cust./Item Disc.
      07.02.01 DFP - Added UL Listing Code
      06.28.01 DFP - Added Width, Length, Thickness fields
                   - Make Class field a lookup
                   - Change to incorporate SP5/e
                   - Change to incorporate Imp 026
                   - Added Wire Size and Wire Type

      06.06.17 ICS - Added "Qty. on Planning Lines" field

      02.27.18 HGR   Added FlowFilter fields "Territory Filter", "State Filter".

                                "Purchasing Dept. Status", "Planning Dept. Status", "E-Ship Dept. Status",
                                "Dimensions Dept. Status", "Item Status Dept. Status".
        WI           07.26.18  Code added in OnDelete Triger for deleting Taxonomy Items.

    }
    END.
  }

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SetBackSlash@4(VAR Value@1000 : Text[250]);
    BEGIN
      IF Value <> '' THEN
        IF Value[STRLEN(Value)] <> '\' THEN
          Value := Value + '\';
    END;

    PROCEDURE ExtractFileName@1000000001(AbsFileName@1000000000 : Text[250];TruncSize@1000000004 : Integer) : Text[250];
    VAR
      ToPos@1000000001 : Integer;
      FromPos@1000000002 : Integer;
      Flag@1000000003 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      Flag := TRUE;
      ToPos := StrLastDotPos(AbsFileName);
      IF ToPos = 0 THEN
        ToPos := STRLEN(AbsFileName) + 1;
      FromPos := ToPos - 1;

      WHILE (FromPos > 1) AND Flag DO
      BEGIN
         IF (AbsFileName[FromPos - 1] = '\') THEN
           Flag := FALSE
         ELSE
           FromPos := FromPos - 1;
      END;

      // Truncate if filename to long
      IF ((ToPos - FromPos) > TruncSize) AND (TruncSize > 0) THEN
        ToPos := FromPos + TruncSize;

      EXIT(COPYSTR(AbsFileName, FromPos,  ToPos - FromPos));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE StrLastDotPos@1000000004(VAR Filename@1000000000 : Text[250]) : Integer;
    VAR
      ToPos@1000000003 : Integer;
      FromPos@1000000002 : Integer;
      Flag@1000000001 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      Flag := TRUE;
      FromPos := STRLEN(Filename);
      WHILE (FromPos > 1) AND Flag DO
      BEGIN
         IF Filename[FromPos] = '.' THEN
           Flag := FALSE
         ELSE
           FromPos := FromPos - 1;
      END;

      IF FromPos = 1 THEN
        FromPos := 0;

      EXIT(FromPos);
    END;

    PROCEDURE ExtractFileExt@1000000007(FileName@1000000000 : Text[250]) : Text[10];
    VAR
      FromPos@1000000002 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      FromPos := StrLastDotPos(FileName);
      IF FromPos > 1 THEN
        EXIT(COPYSTR(FileName, FromPos + 1))
      ELSE
        EXIT('');
    END;

    PROCEDURE ExtractFilePath@1000000003(AbsFileName@1000000000 : Text[250];TruncSize@1000000004 : Integer) : Text[250];
    VAR
      ToPos@1000000001 : Integer;
      FromPos@1000000002 : Integer;
      Flag@1000000003 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      Flag := TRUE;
      ToPos := STRLEN(AbsFileName);

      WHILE (ToPos > 1) AND Flag DO
      BEGIN
         IF (AbsFileName[ToPos] = '\') THEN
           Flag := FALSE
         ELSE
           ToPos := ToPos - 1;
      END;

      // Truncate if filename to long
      IF (ToPos > TruncSize) AND (TruncSize > 0) THEN
        ToPos := TruncSize;

      EXIT(COPYSTR(AbsFileName, 1,  ToPos));
    END;

    PROCEDURE ExtractFileNameAndExt@1000000006(AbsFileName@1000000000 : Text[250];TruncSize@1000000004 : Integer) : Text[250];
    VAR
      ToPos@1000000001 : Integer;
      FromPos@1000000002 : Integer;
      Flag@1000000003 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      Flag := TRUE;
      ToPos := STRLEN(AbsFileName) + 1;
      FromPos := ToPos - 1;

      WHILE (FromPos > 1) AND Flag DO
      BEGIN
         IF (AbsFileName[FromPos - 1] = '\') THEN
           Flag := FALSE
         ELSE
           FromPos := FromPos - 1;
      END;

      // Truncate if filename to long
      IF ((ToPos - FromPos) > TruncSize) AND (TruncSize > 0) THEN
        ToPos := FromPos + TruncSize;

      EXIT(COPYSTR(AbsFileName, FromPos,  ToPos - FromPos));
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Harger customizations (Development by Sbinesh Under VLC Solutions LLC.)                                |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                      |
      ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
        WI          10.02.18  Added fields "Export to website", "FTP Address", "FTP ID", "FTP Password".
    }
    END.
  }

    VAR
      DocumentSetup@1000000006 : Record 50065;
      IMPORTMSG@1000000003 : TextConst 'CSY=Import dokumentu;DAN=Importer Dokument;DEU=Import Dokument;ENU=Import Document;ESP=Importar Documento;NLD=Import Document;NOR=Import Dokument;SVE=Import Dokument;LVI=Import‰t dokumentu;ENG=Import Document;PTG=Importar documento;ENA=Import Document';
      OVERWRITE@1000000002 : TextConst 'CSY=Pýepsat existuj¡c¡ dokument?;DAN=Overskriv eksisterende dokument?;DEU=šberschreiben des exisistierenden Dokuments?;ENU=Overwrite existing document?;ESP=Sobreescribir documento existente?;NLD=Overschrijf bestaand document?;NOR=Skriv over eksisterende dokument?;SVE=Skriv ”ver existerande dokument?;LVI=PƒrrakstŒt esoÕo dokumentu?;ENG=Overwrite existing document?;PTG=Deseja substituir o documento ?;ENA=Overwrite existing document?';
      EXPORT_ERROR@1000000001 : TextConst 'ENU=Error in Exporting File..';

      Text001@1000000011 : TextConst 'ENU=This document is added to multiple Items.\\Do you want to make a Copy for all the Items where this document is added.';
      Text003@1000000010 : TextConst 'ENU=This document is added to multiple Items.Do you want to Continue ?';
      Text004@1000000009 : TextConst 'ENU=Process Cancelled!';
      environment@1000000012 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Environment";

    PROCEDURE Import@1000000000();
    VAR
      FromFileName@1000000003 : Text[1024];
      CommonDlgMgt@1000000002 : Codeunit 412;
      ToFileName@1000000001 : Text[1024];
      StorageGUID@1000000000 : GUID;
      NVIStream@1000000007 : InStream;
      NVOStream@1000000006 : OutStream;
      NVFile@1000000005 : File;
      OK@1000000004 : Boolean;
      DocRecL@1000000008 : Record 50066;
      MultiRec@1000000009 : Boolean;
      FileManagement@1000000010 : Codeunit 419;
    BEGIN
      DocumentSetup.GET;
      CLEAR(MultiRec);

      IF "Table No." = 27 THEN BEGIN
        IF "Ref DocNumber" <> '' THEN
          IF DIALOG.CONFIRM(Text003, FALSE) THEN
            MultiRec := TRUE
          ELSE
            ERROR(Text004);
      END ELSE
       MultiRec := FALSE;

      IF MultiRec THEN BEGIN
        DocRecL.GET("Ref DocNumber");
        WITH DocRecL DO BEGIN               //
          IF "No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
            IF NOT DIALOG.CONFIRM(OVERWRITE, FALSE) THEN
              EXIT;
            IF ISSERVICETIER THEN BEGIN
              IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
                IF UPLOADINTOSTREAM('','','',FromFileName,NVIStream) THEN BEGIN
                  IF CALCFIELDS(Content) THEN
                    OK := Content.HASVALUE;
                  CLEAR(Content);
                  Content.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
                  COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
                  IF NOT OK THEN
                    IF ERASE((DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension")) THEN;
                  CLEAR(GUID);
                END;
              END ELSE
              IF UPLOADINTOSTREAM('','','',FromFileName,NVIStream) THEN BEGIN
                CLEAR(StorageGUID);
                StorageGUID := CREATEGUID();
                ToFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(StorageGUID) +'.'+ DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
                NVFile.CREATE(ToFileName);
                NVFile.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
                COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
                GUID := StorageGUID;
              END;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              OK := FALSE;
              IF CALCFIELDS(Content) THEN
                OK := Content.HASVALUE;
              FromFileName := DocumentSetup.Importpath + '*';
              //>>ICS 05.16.2016
              //FromFileName := CommonDlgMgt.OpenFile(IMPORTMSG, FromFileName, 4, '*.*', 0);
              FromFileName := FileManagement.OpenFileDialog(IMPORTMSG, FromFileName, '*.*');
              //<<
              IF STRPOS(FromFileName,'*') > 0 THEN EXIT; // Cancel
              IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
                CLEAR(Content);
                Content.IMPORT(FromFileName, FALSE);
                IF NOT OK THEN
                  IF ERASE((DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension")) THEN;
                CLEAR(GUID);
              END ELSE BEGIN
                CLEAR(Content);
                CLEAR(StorageGUID);
                StorageGUID := CREATEGUID();
                ToFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(StorageGUID) +'.'+ DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
                IF FILE.COPY(FromFileName,ToFileName) THEN BEGIN
                  IF NOT OK THEN
                    IF ERASE((DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension")) THEN;
                END ELSE
                    ERROR(EXPORT_ERROR);
                GUID := StorageGUID;
              END;
            END;//
              "File Extension" := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
               Description := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileName(FromFileName,0);//doubt abt second parameter
               "Created By" := USERID;
               "Created Date" := WORKDATE;
               MODIFY(TRUE);
          END ELSE BEGIN
            IF ISSERVICETIER THEN BEGIN
              IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
                IF UPLOADINTOSTREAM('','','',FromFileName,NVIStream) THEN BEGIN
                  CLEAR(Content);
                  Content.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
                  COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
                END;
              END ELSE
              IF UPLOADINTOSTREAM('','','',FromFileName,NVIStream) THEN BEGIN
                CLEAR(StorageGUID);
                StorageGUID := CREATEGUID();
                ToFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(StorageGUID) +'.'+ DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
                NVFile.CREATE(ToFileName);
                NVFile.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
                COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
                GUID := StorageGUID;
              END;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              FromFileName := DocumentSetup.Importpath + '*';
              //>>ICS 05.16.2016
              //FromFileName := CommonDlgMgt.OpenFile(IMPORTMSG, FromFileName, 4, '*.*', 0);
              FromFileName := FileManagement.OpenFileDialog(IMPORTMSG, FromFileName, '*.*');
              //<<
              IF STRPOS(FromFileName,'*') > 0 THEN EXIT; // Cancel
              IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
                Content.IMPORT(FromFileName, FALSE);
              END ELSE BEGIN
                CLEAR(StorageGUID);
                StorageGUID := CREATEGUID();
                ToFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(StorageGUID) +'.'+ DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
                IF NOT FILE.COPY(FromFileName,ToFileName) THEN
                  ERROR(EXPORT_ERROR);
                GUID := StorageGUID;
              END;
            END;
            IF EVALUATE("Table No.",GETFILTER("Table No.")) THEN;
            IF GETFILTER("Reference No. 1") <> '' THEN
              "Reference No. 1" := GETFILTER("Reference No. 1");
            IF GETFILTER("Reference No. 2") <> '' THEN
              "Reference No. 2" := GETFILTER("Reference No. 2");
            IF GETFILTER("Reference No. 3") <> '' THEN
              "Reference No. 3" := GETFILTER("Reference No. 3");
            "File Extension" := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
            Description := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileName(FromFileName,0);//doubt abt second parameter
            "Created Date" := WORKDATE;
            "Created By" := USERID;
            INSERT(TRUE);
          END;
        END;                                  //
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF "No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
          IF NOT DIALOG.CONFIRM(OVERWRITE, FALSE) THEN
            EXIT;
          IF ISSERVICETIER THEN BEGIN
            IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
              IF UPLOADINTOSTREAM('','','',FromFileName,NVIStream) THEN BEGIN
                IF CALCFIELDS(Content) THEN
                  OK := Content.HASVALUE;
                CLEAR(Content);
                Content.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
                COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
                IF NOT OK THEN
                  IF ERASE((DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension")) THEN;
                CLEAR(GUID);
              END;
            END ELSE
            IF UPLOADINTOSTREAM('','','',FromFileName,NVIStream) THEN BEGIN
              CLEAR(StorageGUID);
              StorageGUID := CREATEGUID();
              ToFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(StorageGUID) +'.'+ DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
              NVFile.CREATE(ToFileName);
              NVFile.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
              COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
              GUID := StorageGUID;
            END;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            OK := FALSE;
            IF CALCFIELDS(Content) THEN
              OK := Content.HASVALUE;
            FromFileName := DocumentSetup.Importpath + '*';
            //>>ICS 05.16.2016
            //FromFileName := CommonDlgMgt.OpenFile(IMPORTMSG, FromFileName, 4, '*.*', 0);
            FromFileName := FileManagement.OpenFileDialog(IMPORTMSG, FromFileName, '*.*');
            //<<
            IF STRPOS(FromFileName,'*') > 0 THEN EXIT; // Cancel
            IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
              CLEAR(Content);
              Content.IMPORT(FromFileName, FALSE);
              IF NOT OK THEN
                IF ERASE((DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension")) THEN;
              CLEAR(GUID);
            END ELSE BEGIN
              CLEAR(Content);
              CLEAR(StorageGUID);
              StorageGUID := CREATEGUID();
              ToFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(StorageGUID) +'.'+ DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
              IF FILE.COPY(FromFileName,ToFileName) THEN BEGIN
                IF NOT OK THEN
                  IF ERASE((DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension")) THEN;
              END ELSE
                  ERROR(EXPORT_ERROR);
              GUID := StorageGUID;
            END;
          END;
            "File Extension" := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
             Description := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileName(FromFileName,0);//doubt abt second parameter
             "Created By" := USERID;
             "Created Date" := WORKDATE;
             "Ref DocNumber" := '';
             MODIFY(TRUE);
        END ELSE BEGIN
          IF ISSERVICETIER THEN BEGIN
            IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
              IF UPLOADINTOSTREAM('','','',FromFileName,NVIStream) THEN BEGIN
                CLEAR(Content);
                Content.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
                COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
                //MESSAGE('File uploaded!\\%1',FromFileName);
              END;
            END ELSE
            IF UPLOADINTOSTREAM('','','',FromFileName,NVIStream) THEN BEGIN
              CLEAR(StorageGUID);
              StorageGUID := CREATEGUID();
              ToFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(StorageGUID) +'.'+ DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
              NVFile.CREATE(ToFileName);
              NVFile.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
              COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
              GUID := StorageGUID;
            END;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            FromFileName := DocumentSetup.Importpath + '*';
            //>>ICS 05.16.2016
            //FromFileName := CommonDlgMgt.OpenFile(IMPORTMSG, FromFileName, 4, '*.*', 0);
            FromFileName := FileManagement.OpenFileDialog(IMPORTMSG, FromFileName, '*.*');
            //<<
            IF STRPOS(FromFileName,'*') > 0 THEN EXIT; // Cancel
            IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
              Content.IMPORT(FromFileName, FALSE);
            END ELSE BEGIN
              CLEAR(StorageGUID);
              StorageGUID := CREATEGUID();
              ToFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(StorageGUID) +'.'+ DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
              IF NOT FILE.COPY(FromFileName,ToFileName) THEN
                ERROR(EXPORT_ERROR);
              GUID := StorageGUID;
            END;
          END;
          IF EVALUATE("Table No.",GETFILTER("Table No.")) THEN;
          IF GETFILTER("Reference No. 1") <> '' THEN
            "Reference No. 1" := GETFILTER("Reference No. 1");
          IF GETFILTER("Reference No. 2") <> '' THEN
            "Reference No. 2" := GETFILTER("Reference No. 2");
          IF GETFILTER("Reference No. 3") <> '' THEN
            "Reference No. 3" := GETFILTER("Reference No. 3");
          "File Extension" := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileExt(FromFileName);
          Description := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileName(FromFileName,0);//doubt abt second parameter
          "Created Date" := WORKDATE;
          "Created By" := USERID;
          "Ref DocNumber" := '';
          INSERT(TRUE);
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CopyDoc@1000000001();
    VAR
      Doc@1000000000 : Record 50066;
      NewGUID@1000000003 : GUID;
      FromFileName@1000000002 : Text[1024];
      ToFileName@1000000001 : Text[1024];
      tempFile@1000000004 : Text[1024];
      OK@1000000005 : Boolean;
      NVIStream@1000000010 : InStream;
      NVOStream@1000000009 : OutStream;
      NVFile@1000000008 : File;
    BEGIN
      Doc.RESET;
      DocumentSetup.GET;
      OK := FALSE;
      IF CALCFIELDS(Content) THEN
        OK := Content.HASVALUE;
      IF "No." = '' THEN
        ERROR(DOC_ERROR);
      Doc.COPY(Rec);
      Doc."No." := '';
      NewGUID := CREATEGUID();
      ToFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(NewGUID) +'.'+ "File Extension";
      IF NOT OK THEN BEGIN
        FromFileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension";
        //
        IF ISSERVICETIER THEN BEGIN
          IF NOT dnFile.Exists(FromFileName) THEN BEGIN
            MESSAGE(DOC_ERROR);
            EXIT;
          END;
        END ELSE BEGIN
        //
          IF NOT FILE.EXISTS(FromFileName) THEN BEGIN
            MESSAGE(DOC_ERROR);
            EXIT;
          END;
        END;  //
      END;
      IF ISSERVICETIER THEN BEGIN
        IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
          IF OK THEN BEGIN
            CLEAR(Doc.GUID);
            Content.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
            Doc.Content.CREATEINSTREAM(NVIStream);
            COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
            Doc."Created Date" := WORKDATE;
            Doc."Created By" := USERID;
            CLEAR(Doc.GUID);
            Doc.INSERT(TRUE);
          END ELSE BEGIN
            //
            dnFile.Delete('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
            dnFile.Copy(FromFileName,'\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
            NVFile.OPEN('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
            //NVFile.OPEN(FromFileName);
            //
            NVFile.CREATEINSTREAM(NVIStream);
            Doc.Content.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
            COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
            Doc."Created Date" := WORKDATE;
            Doc."Created By" := USERID;
            CLEAR(Doc.GUID);
            Doc.INSERT(TRUE);
            NVFile.CLOSE;
            dnFile.Delete('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension"); //
          END;
        END ELSE BEGIN
          IF OK THEN BEGIN
            CLEAR(Doc.Content);
            CLEAR(Doc.GUID);
            Content.CREATEINSTREAM(NVIStream);
            NVFile.CREATE(ToFileName);
            NVFile.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
            COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
            Doc.GUID := NewGUID;
            Doc."Created Date" := WORKDATE;
            Doc."Created By" := USERID;
            Doc.INSERT(TRUE);
          END ELSE BEGIN
            CLEAR(Doc.GUID);
            CLEAR(Doc.Content);
            //
            dnFile.Delete('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
            dnFile.Copy(FromFileName,'\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
            NVFile.OPEN('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
            //NVFile.OPEN(FromFileName);
            //
            NVFile.CREATEINSTREAM(NVIStream);
            NVFile.CLOSE;
            //NVFile.CREATE(ToFileName);
            //NVFile.CLOSE;
            //NVFile.WRITEMODE(TRUE);
            //
            dnFile.Delete('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
            dnFile.Copy(ToFileName,'\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
            NVFile.OPEN('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
            //NVFile.OPEN(ToFileName);
            //
            NVFile.CREATEOUTSTREAM(NVOStream);
            COPYSTREAM(NVOStream,NVIStream);
            Doc.GUID := NewGUID;
            Doc."Created Date" := WORKDATE;
            Doc."Created By" := USERID;
            Doc.INSERT(TRUE);
            NVFile.CLOSE;
            dnFile.Delete('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");  //
          END;
        END;
      END ELSE
      IF NOT DocumentSetup."Enable External Storage" THEN BEGIN
        IF OK THEN BEGIN
            CALCFIELDS(Content);
            Doc.Content := Content;
        END ELSE
          Doc.Content.IMPORT(FromFileName,FALSE);
        CLEAR(Doc.GUID);
        Doc."Created Date" := WORKDATE;
        Doc."Created By" := USERID;
        Doc.INSERT(TRUE);
      END ELSE
        IF OK THEN BEGIN
          Content.EXPORT(ToFileName,FALSE);
          //CALCFIELDS(Doc.Content);
          CLEAR(Doc.Content);
          Doc.GUID := NewGUID;
          Doc."Created Date" := WORKDATE;
          Doc."Created By" := USERID;
          Doc.INSERT(TRUE);
        END ELSE
          IF FILE.COPY(FromFileName,ToFileName) THEN BEGIN
           //CALCFIELDS(Doc.Content);
            CLEAR(Doc.Content);
            Doc.GUID := NewGUID;
            Doc."Created Date" := WORKDATE;
            Doc."Created By" := USERID;
            Doc.INSERT(TRUE);
          END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE Print@1000000002();
    VAR
      Path@1000000002 : Text[250];
      Name@1000000001 : Text[250];
      FromFile@1000000004 : Text[1024];
      OK@1000000006 : Boolean;
      ExportFile@1000000000 : Text[1024];
      NVFile@1000000003 : File;
      NVIStream@1000000005 : InStream;
      NVOStream@1000000007 : OutStream;
      TempFile@1000000008 : Text[1024];
    BEGIN
      DocumentSetup.GET;
      ExportFile := Description + '.' + "File Extension";
      IF CALCFIELDS(Content) THEN
        OK := Content.HASVALUE;

      IF ISSERVICETIER THEN BEGIN
        IF OK THEN BEGIN
          Content.CREATEINSTREAM(NVIStream);
          IF NOT DOWNLOADFROMSTREAM(NVIStream,'','<TEMP>','',ExportFile) THEN
            ERROR('No Document');
          Path := DocumentSetup.ExtractFilePath(ExportFile,0);
          Name := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileNameAndExt(ExportFile,0);
        END ELSE BEGIN
          FromFile:= DocumentSetup.Externalpath + '\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension";
          //
          dnFile.Delete('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
          dnFile.Copy(FromFile,'\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
          NVFile.OPEN('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
          //NVFile.OPEN(FromFile); \\GR-NAV2009\temp\
          //
          NVFile.CREATEINSTREAM(NVIStream);
          IF NOT DOWNLOADFROMSTREAM(NVIStream,'','<TEMP>','',ExportFile) THEN
            ERROR('No Document');
          Path := DocumentSetup.ExtractFilePath(ExportFile,0);
          Name := DocumentSetup.ExtractFileNameAndExt(ExportFile,0);
          dnFile.Delete('\\GR-NAV2009\temp\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
        END;

        DocManagement.Print(Path,Name);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF OK THEN BEGIN
          //TempFile := ENVIRON('temp') + '\' + Description + '.' + "File Extension";
          TempFile := environment.GetEnvironmentVariable('temp') + '\' + Description + '.' + "File Extension";
          Content.EXPORT(TempFile);
          //Path := ENVIRON('temp') + '\';
          Path := environment.GetEnvironmentVariable('temp') + '\';
          Name := Description + '.' + "File Extension";
        END ELSE BEGIN
          FromFile:= DocumentSetup.Externalpath + '\' + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension";
          //TempFile := ENVIRON('temp') + '\' + Description + '.' + "File Extension";
          TempFile := environment.GetEnvironmentVariable('temp') + '\' + Description + '.' + "File Extension";
          IF NOT FILE.COPY(FromFile,TempFile) THEN BEGIN
            MESSAGE(DOC_ERROR);
            EXIT;
          END;
          //Path := ENVIRON('temp') + '\';
          Path := environment.GetEnvironmentVariable('temp') + '\';
          Name := Description + '.' + "File Extension";
        END;
        TempFile := Path + Name;
        IF EXISTS(TempFile) THEN BEGIN
          DocManagement.Print(Path,Name);
        END ELSE
          ERROR('No Document');
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetupNew@1();
    VAR
      NoSerieMgnt@1000 : Codeunit 396;
    BEGIN
      IF ("No." = '') THEN
        BEGIN
          DocumentSetup.GET;
          DocumentSetup.TESTFIELD("Document Nos.");
          NoSerieMgnt.InitSeries(DocumentSetup."Document Nos.",'',0D,"No.",DocumentSetup."Document Nos.");
        END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE MailAdr@12() : Text[80];
    VAR
      CustomerRec@1000000011 : Record 18;
      VendorRec@1000000010 : Record 23;
      ContactRec@1000000008 : Record 5050;
      EmployeeRec@1000000007 : Record 5200;
      BankRec@1000000012 : Record 270;
    BEGIN
      IF "Reference No. 1" = '' THEN
        EXIT('');

      CASE "Table No." OF
        18:
          IF CustomerRec.GET("Reference No. 1") THEN
            EXIT(CustomerRec."E-Mail");

        23:
          IF VendorRec.GET("Reference No. 1") THEN
            EXIT(VendorRec."E-Mail");

        5200:
          IF EmployeeRec.GET("Reference No. 1") THEN
            EXIT(EmployeeRec."E-Mail");

        5050:
          IF ContactRec.GET("Reference No. 1") THEN
            EXIT(ContactRec."E-Mail");

         270:
          IF BankRec.GET("Reference No. 1") THEN
            EXIT(BankRec."E-Mail");

      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE Send@14();
    VAR
      FileName@1000000000 : Text[250];
      Mail@1001 : Codeunit 397;
      TempFile@1000000001 : Text[1024];
      ClientFileName@1000000004 : Text[250];
      ToFile@1000000005 : Text[250];
      OK@1000000007 : Boolean;
      ToPath@1000000008 : Text;
    BEGIN
      DocumentSetup.GET;
      IF CALCFIELDS(Content) THEN
        OK := Content.HASVALUE;
      CLEAR(NVFile);
      IF ISSERVICETIER THEN BEGIN
        IF OK THEN BEGIN
          Content.CREATEINSTREAM(NVIStream);
          DOWNLOADFROMSTREAM(NVIStream,'','<TEMP>','',TempFile);
        END ELSE BEGIN
          FileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension";
          dnFile.Delete(DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
          dnFile.Copy(FileName,DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
          IF NOT NVFile.OPEN(DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension") THEN
          //IF NOT NVFile.OPEN(FileName) THEN
            ERROR('No access to external file');
          NVFile.CREATEINSTREAM(NVIStream);
          IF NOT DOWNLOADFROMSTREAM(NVIStream,'','<TEMP>','',TempFile) THEN
            ERROR('not downloaded');
          //NVFile.CLOSE;
          dnFile.Delete(DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension");
        END;
          ToFile := Description+ '.' + "File Extension";
          ToPath := FORMAT( FileMgt.GetDirectoryName(TempFile))+'\'+COPYSTR(FORMAT(CREATEGUID),1,38);
          FileMgt.CreateClientDirectory(ToPath);
          FileMgt.MoveAndRenameClientFile(TempFile,ToFile,ToPath);
          ClientFileName := ToPath+'\'+ToFile;
          // create mails with this attachment
          Mail.NewMessage(MailAdr,'','',Description,'',ClientFileName, TRUE);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        //TempFile := ENVIRON('TEMP') +'\'+ Description+ '.' + "File Extension";
        TempFile := environment.GetEnvironmentVariable('TEMP') +'\'+ Description+ '.' + "File Extension";
        IF OK THEN
          Content.EXPORT(TempFile,FALSE)
        ELSE BEGIN
          FileName := DocumentSetup.Externalpath + FORMAT(GUID) + '.' + "File Extension";
          IF NOT FILE.COPY(FileName,TempFile) THEN BEGIN
            ERROR(DOC_ERROR);
            EXIT;
          END;
        END;
        //create mails with this attachment
        IF EXISTS(TempFile) THEN BEGIN
          Mail.NewMessage(MailAdr,'','',Description,'',ClientFileName, TRUE);
          FILE.ERASE(TempFile);
        END ELSE
          ERROR('File Does not Exists');
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE View@1000000003(VAR DocMgt@1000000000 : Codeunit 50000);

      DocRecL@1000000001 : Record 50066;

    END;

    PROCEDURE Export@1000000005();

    END;

    PROCEDURE ServerTempFileName@5() FileName : Text[1024];

    END;

    PROCEDURE WhereUsed@1000000006();
    VAR
      DocRecL@1000000000 : Record 50066;
      POS@1000000001 : Integer;
      DocForm@1000000002 : Page 50122;
    BEGIN
      POS := STRPOS("Ref DocNumber",'DOC');
      DocRecL.RESET;
      IF POS <> 0 THEN
        DocRecL.SETRANGE(DocRecL."Ref DocNumber","Ref DocNumber")
      ELSE
        DocRecL.SETRANGE(DocRecL."No.","No.");
      DocForm.SETTABLEVIEW(DocRecL);
      IF DocForm.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
        DocForm.GETRECORD(DocRecL);
    END;

    PROCEDURE ViewSourceDoc@1000000007();
    VAR
      DocForm@1000000000 : Page 50122;
      DocRecL@1000000001 : Record 50066;
    BEGIN
      {
      DocRecL.RESET;
      IF "Ref DocNumber" <> '' THEN
        DocRecL.SETRANGE(DocRecL."No.","Ref DocNumber")
      ELSE
        DocRecL.SETRANGE(DocRecL."No.","No.");
      DocForm.SETTABLEVIEW(DocRecL);
      IF DocForm.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
        DocForm.GETRECORD(DocRecL);
      }
      DocRecL.RESET;
      IF "Ref DocNumber" <> '' THEN BEGIN
        DocRecL.SETRANGE(DocRecL."No.","Ref DocNumber");
      //ELSE
      //  DocRecL.SETRANGE(DocRecL."No.","No.");
        DocForm.SETTABLEVIEW(DocRecL);
        IF DocForm.RUNMODAL = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
          DocForm.GETRECORD(DocRecL);
      END;
    END;
