    LOCAL PROCEDURE SendItemsToWebsite@1000000009(TypeP@1000000001 : 'Create,Update,Delete');
    VAR
      SendItems@1000000000 : Record 50104;
      Item@1000000002 : Record 27;
    BEGIN
      //>>WI 10.04.18
        SendItems.RESET;
        SendItems.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Document No.","File Extension");
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","Reference No. 1");
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Document No.", "No.");
        SendItems.SETRANGE("File Extension", "File Extension");
        IF TypeP = TypeP::Create THEN
          SendItems.SETRANGE(Type, SendItems.Type::Create)
        ELSE IF TypeP = TypeP::Update THEN
          SendItems.SETRANGE(Type, SendItems.Type::Update)
        ELSE IF TypeP = TypeP::Delete THEN
          SendItems.SETRANGE(Type, SendItems.Type::Delete);
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Process Status",SendItems."Process Status"::Pending);
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Product Type", SendItems."Product Type"::Documents);
        IF SendItems.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
          SendItems.INIT;
          SendItems."Entry No." := 0;
          SendItems."Item No." := "Reference No. 1";
          SendItems.Type := TypeP;
          SendItems."Product Type" := SendItems."Product Type"::Documents;
          SendItems."Process Status" := SendItems."Process Status"::Pending;
          SendItems."Inserted By" := USERID;
          SendItems."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
          SendItems."Document No." := "No.";
          SendItems."File Extension" := "File Extension";
          SendItems.INSERT(TRUE);
        END;
      //<<WI 10.04.18
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DeleteSendItemsToWebsite@1000000008();
    VAR
      SendItems@1000000000 : Record 50104;
    BEGIN
      //>>WI 10.04.18
        SendItems.RESET;
        SendItems.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Document No.","File Extension");
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","Reference No. 1");
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Document No.", "No.");
        SendItems.SETRANGE("File Extension", "File Extension");
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Product Type", SendItems."Product Type"::Documents);
        SendItems.DELETEALL;
      //<<WI 10.04.18
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      +-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Harger Customizations (Development by Sbinesh Under VLC Solutions LLC.)                                     |
      +-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                           |
      --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
        HGR         06.01.18  Replace the ENVIRON function to environment.GetEnvironmentVariable [DotNet Variable]
        HGR         06.01.18  Replace the CommonDlgMgt.OpenFile to FileManagement.OpenFileDialog [Codeunit 419]
        WI          10.04.18  Added field "Sent to Website" and relate Code for sending document to website.
    }
    END.
  }
}

OBJECT Table 50081 Item Catalog Entry
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=10/23/18;
    Time=[ 5:25:31 AM];
    Modified=Yes;
    Version List=Entry No AutoIncr yes,WI;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    OnInsert=BEGIN
               //>>WI 10.10.18
               IF "Catalog Code" = 'WEBSITE' THEN
                 IF Item.GET("Item No.") THEN
                   CheckToSendtoWebsite(0,TRUE);
               //<<WI 10.10.18
             END;

    OnModify=BEGIN
               //>>WI 10.10.18
               IF (xRec."Catalog Code" = 'WEBSITE') AND ("Catalog Code" <> 'WEBSITE') THEN BEGIN
                 IF Item.GET("Item No.") THEN
                   CheckToSendtoWebsite(2,TRUE);
               END ELSE BEGIN
                 IF "Catalog Code" = 'WEBSITE' THEN
                   IF Item.GET("Item No.") THEN
                     CheckToSendtoWebsite(0,TRUE);
               END;
               //<<WI 10.10.18
             END;

    OnDelete=BEGIN
               //>>WI 10.10.18
               IF "Catalog Code" = 'WEBSITE' THEN
                 IF Item.GET("Item No.") THEN
                   CheckToSendtoWebsite(2,TRUE);
               //<<WI 10.10.18

    PROCEDURE CheckToSendtoWebsite@1000000011(TypeP@1000000000 : 'Create,Update,Delete';ExternalP@1000000002 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SendItems@1000000001 : Record 50104;
      ItemCatalogEntry@1000000003 : Record 50081;
    BEGIN
      //>>WI 09.17.18
      IF TypeP <> 2 THEN BEGIN
        IF ExternalP THEN BEGIN
          SendItems.RESET;
          SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
          SendItems.SETRANGE(Type,TypeP);
          SendItems.SETRANGE("Process Status",SendItems."Process Status"::" ");
          IF SendItems.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            SendItems.RESET;
            SendItems.INIT;
            SendItems."Entry No." := 0;
            SendItems."Item No." := "Item No.";
            SendItems."Inserted By" := USERID;
            SendItems."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
            IF ExternalP AND (Item.SkuID <> '') THEN
              SendItems.Type := SendItems.Type::Update
            ELSE
              SendItems.Type := TypeP;
            SendItems."Product Type" := SendItems."Product Type"::Product;
            SendItems.INSERT(TRUE);
          END;
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        SendItems.RESET;
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
        SendItems.SETFILTER(Type,'<>%1',TypeP);
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Process Status",SendItems."Process Status"::" ");
        IF NOT SendItems.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
          SendItems.DELETEALL;
        END;
        IF Item.SkuID <> '' THEN BEGIN
          SendItems.RESET;
          SendItems.INIT;
          SendItems."Entry No." := 0;
          SendItems."Item No." := "Item No.";
          SendItems."Inserted By" := USERID;
          SendItems."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
          SendItems.Type := TypeP;
          SendItems."Product Type" := SendItems."Product Type"::Product;
          SendItems.INSERT(TRUE);
        END;
      END;
      //<<WI 09.17.18
    END;

    BEGIN
    {

      | Harger Customizations   (Development by Sbinesh Under VLC Solutions LLC.)                              |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                      |
      ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
        WI          10.10.18  Added Code.
    }
    END.

  {
    VAR
      ItemSpecification@1000000000 : Record 50088;
      ItemG@1000000002 : Record 27;
      ItemLenG@1000000001 : Integer;
      SalesReceivablesSetup@1000000003 : Record 311;

    PROCEDURE CheckToSendtoWebsite@1000000011(TypeP@1000000000 : 'Create,Update,Delete';ExternalP@1000000002 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SendItems@1000000001 : Record 50104;
      ItemCatalogEntry@1000000003 : Record 50081;
    BEGIN
      //>>WI 09.17.18
      IF TypeP <> 2 THEN BEGIN
        IF ("Note 1" <> xRec."Note 1") OR
          ("Note 2" <> xRec."Note 2") OR
          ("Note 3" <> xRec."Note 3") OR
          ("Note 4" <> xRec."Note 4") OR
          ("Note 5" <> xRec."Note 5") OR
          ("Note 6" <> xRec."Note 6") OR
          ("Note 7" <> xRec."Note 7") OR
          ("Note 8" <> xRec."Note 8") OR
          ("Technical 1" <> xRec."Technical 1") OR
          ("Technical 2" <> xRec."Technical 2") OR
          ("Technical 3" <> xRec."Technical 3") OR
          ("Technical 4" <> xRec."Technical 4") OR
          ("Technical 5" <> xRec."Technical 5") OR
          ("Technical 6" <> xRec."Technical 6") OR
          ("Technical 7" <> xRec."Technical 7") OR
          ("Technical 8" <> xRec."Technical 8") OR
          ("Application 1" <> xRec."Application 1") OR
          ("Application 2" <> xRec."Application 2") OR
          ("Application 3" <> xRec."Application 3") OR
          ("Application 4" <> xRec."Application 4") OR
          ("Application 5" <> xRec."Application 5") OR
          ("Application 6" <> xRec."Application 6") OR
          ("Application 7" <> xRec."Application 7") OR
          ("Application 8" <> xRec."Application 8") OR
          ("UNSPSC Code" <> xRec."UNSPSC Code") OR
          ("Image URL" <> xRec."UNSPSC Code") OR
          (ExternalP) THEN BEGIN
            ItemCatalogEntry.RESET;
            ItemCatalogEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Catalog Code");
            ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
            ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Catalog Code",'WEBSITE');
            IF NOT ItemCatalogEntry.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
              SendItems.RESET;
              SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
              SendItems.SETRANGE(Type,TypeP);
              SendItems.SETRANGE("Process Status",SendItems."Process Status"::" ");
              IF SendItems.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                SendItems.RESET;
                SendItems.INIT;
                SendItems."Entry No." := 0;
                SendItems."Item No." := "Item No.";
                SendItems."Inserted By" := USERID;
                SendItems."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
                IF ExternalP AND (ItemG.SkuID <> '') THEN
                  SendItems.Type := SendItems.Type::Update
                ELSE
                  SendItems.Type := TypeP;
                SendItems.INSERT(TRUE);
              END;
            END;
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        SendItems.RESET;
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
        SendItems.SETFILTER(Type,'<>%1',TypeP);
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Process Status",SendItems."Process Status"::" ");
        IF NOT SendItems.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
          SendItems.DELETEALL;
        END;
        IF ItemG.SkuID <> '' THEN BEGIN
          ItemCatalogEntry.RESET;
          ItemCatalogEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Catalog Code");
          ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
          ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Catalog Code",'WEBSITE');
          IF NOT ItemCatalogEntry.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            SendItems.RESET;
            SendItems.INIT;
            SendItems."Entry No." := 0;
            SendItems."Item No." := "Item No.";
            SendItems."Inserted By" := USERID;
            SendItems."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
            SendItems.Type := TypeP;
            SendItems.INSERT(TRUE);
          END;
        END;
      END;
      //<<WI 09.17.18
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      +----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Harger Customizations   (Development by Sbinesh Under VLC Solutions LLC.)                                      |
      +----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                              |
      -----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
        WI         09.17.18  Added Code.
    }
    END.
  }

    PROCEDURE Load@1(StreamOrServerFile@1002 : Variant);
    VAR
      XMLBufferWriter@1000 : Codeunit 50057;
    BEGIN
      XMLBufferWriter.InitializeXMLBufferFrom(Rec,StreamOrServerFile);
    END;

    PROCEDURE LoadFromText@10(XmlText@1001 : Text);
    VAR
      XMLBufferWriter@1000 : Codeunit 50057;
    BEGIN
      XMLBufferWriter.InitializeXMLBufferFromText(Rec,XmlText);
    END;

    PROCEDURE Upload@12() : Boolean;
    VAR
      FileManagement@1000 : Codeunit 419;
      ServerTempFileName@1001 : Text;
    BEGIN
      ServerTempFileName := FileManagement.UploadFile('','*.xml');
      IF ServerTempFileName = '' THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      Load(ServerTempFileName);
      FileManagement.DeleteServerFile(ServerTempFileName);
      EXIT(TRUE);
    END;

    PROCEDURE Save@38(ServerFilePath@1000 : Text) : Boolean;
    VAR
      XMLBufferReader@1002 : Codeunit 50058;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(XMLBufferReader.SaveToFile(ServerFilePath,Rec));
    END;

    PROCEDURE Download@13() Success : Boolean;
    VAR
      FileManagement@1000 : Codeunit 419;
      ServerTempFileName@1001 : Text;
    BEGIN
      ServerTempFileName := FileManagement.ServerTempFileName('xml');
      Save(ServerTempFileName);
      Success := FileManagement.DownloadHandler(ServerTempFileName,'','','','temp.xml');
      FileManagement.DeleteServerFile(ServerTempFileName);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateRootElement@23(ElementName@1000 : Text[250]);
    VAR
      XMLBufferWriter@1001 : Codeunit 50057;
    BEGIN
      XMLBufferWriter.InsertElement(Rec,Rec,1,1,ElementName,'');
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddNamespace@14(NamespacePrefix@1000 : Text[244];NamespacePath@1001 : Text[250]);
    BEGIN
      IF NamespacePrefix = '' THEN
        AddAttribute('xmlns',NamespacePath)
      ELSE
        AddAttribute('xmlns:' + NamespacePrefix,NamespacePath);
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddAttribute@7(AttributeName@1001 : Text[250];AttributeValue@1000 : Text[250]);
    VAR
      XMLBufferWriter@1002 : Codeunit 50057;
    BEGIN
      XMLBufferWriter.InsertAttribute(Rec,Rec,CountAttributes + 1,Depth + 1,AttributeName,AttributeValue);
      GetParent;
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddGroupElement@3(ElementNameWithNamespace@1001 : Text[250]) : Integer;
    VAR
      XMLBufferWriter@1000 : Codeunit 50057;
    BEGIN
      XMLBufferWriter.InsertElement(Rec,Rec,CountChildElements + 1,Depth + 1,ElementNameWithNamespace,'');
      EXIT("Entry No.");
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddGroupElementAt@18(ElementNameWithNamespace@1003 : Text[250];EntryNo@1000 : Integer) : Integer;
    VAR
      XMLBufferWriter@1002 : Codeunit 50057;
      CurrentView@1004 : Text;
      ElementNo@1001 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      CurrentView := GETVIEW;
      GET(EntryNo);
      ElementNo := "Node Number";
      RESET;
      SETRANGE("Parent Entry No.","Parent Entry No.");
      SETFILTER("Node Number",'>=%1',ElementNo);
      IF FINDSET(TRUE) THEN
        REPEAT
          "Node Number" += 1;
          MODIFY;
        UNTIL NEXT = 0;
      GET("Parent Entry No.");
      XMLBufferWriter.InsertElement(Rec,Rec,ElementNo,Depth + 1,ElementNameWithNamespace,'');
      SETVIEW(CurrentView);
      EXIT("Entry No.");
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddElement@5(ElementNameWithNamespace@1007 : Text[250];ElementValue@1006 : Text[250]) ElementEntryNo : Integer;
    BEGIN
      ElementEntryNo := AddGroupElement(ElementNameWithNamespace);
      Value := ElementValue;
      MODIFY(TRUE);
      GetParent;
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddLastElement@6(ElementNameWithNamespace@1001 : Text[250];ElementValue@1000 : Text[250]) ElementEntryNo : Integer;
    BEGIN
      ElementEntryNo := AddElement(ElementNameWithNamespace,ElementValue);
      GetParent;
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddNonEmptyElement@15(ElementNameWithNamespace@1007 : Text[250];ElementValue@1006 : Text[250]) ElementEntryNo : Integer;
    BEGIN
      IF ElementValue = '' THEN
        EXIT;
      ElementEntryNo := AddElement(ElementNameWithNamespace,ElementValue);
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddNonEmptyLastElement@17(ElementNameWithNamespace@1007 : Text[250];ElementValue@1006 : Text[250]) ElementEntryNo : Integer;
    BEGIN
      ElementEntryNo := AddNonEmptyElement(ElementNameWithNamespace,ElementValue);
      GetParent;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CopyImportFrom@9(VAR TempXMLBuffer@1001 : TEMPORARY Record 50097);
    VAR
      XMLBuffer@1000 : Record 50097;
    BEGIN
      IF TempXMLBuffer.ISTEMPORARY THEN
        COPY(TempXMLBuffer,TRUE)
      ELSE BEGIN
        XMLBuffer.SETRANGE("Import ID",TempXMLBuffer."Import ID");
        IF XMLBuffer.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            Rec := XMLBuffer;
            INSERT;
          UNTIL XMLBuffer.NEXT = 0;
        SETVIEW(TempXMLBuffer.GETVIEW);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CountChildElements@37() NumElements : Integer;
    VAR
      CurrentView@1002 : Text;
    BEGIN
      CurrentView := GETVIEW;
      RESET;
      SETRANGE("Parent Entry No.","Entry No.");
      SETRANGE(Type,Type::Element);
      NumElements := COUNT;
      SETVIEW(CurrentView);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CountAttributes@43() NumAttributes : Integer;
    VAR
      CurrentView@1002 : Text;
    BEGIN
      CurrentView := GETVIEW;
      RESET;
      SETRANGE("Parent Entry No.","Entry No.");
      SETRANGE(Type,Type::Attribute);
      NumAttributes := COUNT;
      SETVIEW(CurrentView);
    END;

    PROCEDURE FindAttributes@19(VAR TempResultAttributeXMLBuffer@1000 : TEMPORARY Record 50097) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(FindChildNodes(TempResultAttributeXMLBuffer,Type::Attribute,''));
    END;

    PROCEDURE FindChildElements@16(VAR TempResultElementXMLBuffer@1000 : TEMPORARY Record 50097) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(FindChildNodes(TempResultElementXMLBuffer,Type::Element,''));
    END;

    PROCEDURE FindNodesByXPath@2(VAR TempResultElementXMLBuffer@1000 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;XPath@1002 : Text) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      TempResultElementXMLBuffer.CopyImportFrom(Rec);

      TempResultElementXMLBuffer.SETRANGE("Import ID","Import ID");
      TempResultElementXMLBuffer.SETRANGE("Parent Entry No.");
      TempResultElementXMLBuffer.SETFILTER(Path,'*' + XPath);
      EXIT(TempResultElementXMLBuffer.FINDSET);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetAttributeValue@50(AttributeName@1000 : Text) : Text[250];
    VAR
      TempXMLBuffer@1002 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;
    BEGIN
      IF FindChildNodes(TempXMLBuffer,Type::Attribute,AttributeName) THEN
        EXIT(TempXMLBuffer.Value);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetElementName@68() : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF Namespace = '' THEN
        EXIT(Name);
      EXIT(Namespace + ':' + Name);
    END;

    [TryFunction]
    PROCEDURE GetParent@8();
    BEGIN
      GET("Parent Entry No.");
    END;

    PROCEDURE HasChildNodes@4() ChildNodesExists : Boolean;
    VAR
      CurrentView@1002 : Text;
    BEGIN
      CurrentView := GETVIEW;
      RESET;
      SETRANGE("Parent Entry No.","Entry No.");
      ChildNodesExists := NOT ISEMPTY;
      SETVIEW(CurrentView);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE FindChildNodes@11(VAR TempResultXMLBuffer@1003 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;NodeType@1000 : Option;NodeName@1001 : Text) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      TempResultXMLBuffer.CopyImportFrom(Rec);

      TempResultXMLBuffer.SETRANGE("Parent Entry No.","Entry No.");
      TempResultXMLBuffer.SETRANGE(Path);
      TempResultXMLBuffer.SETRANGE(Type,NodeType);
      IF NodeName <> '' THEN
        TempResultXMLBuffer.SETRANGE(Name,NodeName);
      EXIT(TempResultXMLBuffer.FINDSET);
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Harger Customizations   (Development by Sbinesh Under VLC Solutions LLC.)                              |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                      |
      ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
        WI         03.29.18  Added new object for XML buffer.
    }
    END.
  }

    PROCEDURE CheckToSendtoWebsite@1000000011(TypeP@1000000000 : 'Create,Update,Delete';ExternalP@1000000002 : Boolean);
    VAR
      SendItems@1000000001 : Record 50104;
      ItemCatalogEntry@1000000003 : Record 50081;
    BEGIN
      //>>WI 09.17.18
      IF TypeP <> 2 THEN BEGIN
        IF ("Level 1" <> xRec."Level 1") OR
          ("Level 2" <> xRec."Level 2") OR
          ("Level 3" <> xRec."Level 3") OR
          ("Level 4" <> xRec."Level 4") OR
          ("Level 5" <> xRec."Level 5") OR
          ("Level 6" <> xRec."Level 6") OR
          ("Level 7" <> xRec."Level 7") OR
          ("Level 8" <> xRec."Level 8") OR
          ("Level 9" <> xRec."Level 9") OR
          ("Level 10" <> xRec."Level 10") OR
          ("Attribute 1" <> xRec."Attribute 1") OR
          ("Attribute 2" <> xRec."Attribute 2") OR
          ("Attribute 3" <> xRec."Attribute 3") OR
          ("Attribute 4" <> xRec."Attribute 4") OR
          ("Attribute 5" <> xRec."Attribute 5") OR
          ("Attribute 6" <> xRec."Attribute 6") OR
          ("Attribute 7" <> xRec."Attribute 7") OR
          ("Attribute 8" <> xRec."Attribute 8") OR
          ("Attribute 9" <> xRec."Attribute 9") OR
          ("Attribute 10" <> xRec."Attribute 10") OR
          ("Attribute 11" <> xRec."Attribute 11") OR
          ("Attribute 12" <> xRec."Attribute 12") OR
          ("Attribute 13" <> xRec."Attribute 13") OR
          ("Attribute 14" <> xRec."Attribute 14") OR
          ("Attribute 15" <> xRec."Attribute 15") OR
          ("Attribute 16" <> xRec."Attribute 16") OR
          ("Attribute 17" <> xRec."Attribute 17") OR
          ("Attribute 18" <> xRec."Attribute 18") OR
          ("Attribute 19" <> xRec."Attribute 19") OR
          ("Attribute 20" <> xRec."Attribute 20") OR
          ("Attribute 21" <> xRec."Attribute 21") OR
          ("Attribute 22" <> xRec."Attribute 22") OR
          ("Attribute 23" <> xRec."Attribute 23") OR
          ("Attribute 24" <> xRec."Attribute 24") OR
          ("Attribute 25" <> xRec."Attribute 25") OR
          ("Attribute 26" <> xRec."Attribute 26") OR
          ("Attribute 27" <> xRec."Attribute 27") OR
          ("Attribute 28" <> xRec."Attribute 28") OR
          ("Value 1" <> xRec."Value 1") OR
          ("Value 2" <> xRec."Value 2") OR
          ("Value 3" <> xRec."Value 3") OR
          ("Value 4" <> xRec."Value 4") OR
          ("Value 5" <> xRec."Value 5") OR
          ("Value 6" <> xRec."Value 6") OR
          ("Value 7" <> xRec."Value 7") OR
          ("Value 8" <> xRec."Value 8") OR
          ("Value 9" <> xRec."Value 9") OR
          ("Value 10" <> xRec."Value 10") OR
          ("Value 11" <> xRec."Value 11") OR
          ("Value 12" <> xRec."Value 12") OR
          ("Value 13" <> xRec."Value 13") OR
          ("Value 14" <> xRec."Value 14") OR
          ("Value 15" <> xRec."Value 16") OR
          ("Value 16" <> xRec."Value 16") OR
          ("Value 17" <> xRec."Value 17") OR
          ("Value 18" <> xRec."Value 18") OR
          ("Value 19" <> xRec."Value 19") OR
          ("Value 20" <> xRec."Value 20") OR
          ("Value 21" <> xRec."Value 21") OR
          ("Value 22" <> xRec."Value 22") OR
          ("Value 23" <> xRec."Value 23") OR
          ("Value 24" <> xRec."Value 24") OR
          ("Value 25" <> xRec."Value 25") OR
          ("Value 26" <> xRec."Value 26") OR
          ("Value 27" <> xRec."Value 27") OR
          ("Value 28" <> xRec."Value 28") OR
          (ExternalP) THEN BEGIN
            ItemCatalogEntry.RESET;
            ItemCatalogEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Catalog Code");
            ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
            ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Catalog Code",'WEBSITE');
            IF NOT ItemCatalogEntry.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
              SendItems.RESET;
              SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
              SendItems.SETRANGE(Type,TypeP);
              SendItems.SETRANGE("Process Status",SendItems."Process Status"::" ");
              IF SendItems.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                SendItems.RESET;
                SendItems.INIT;
                SendItems."Entry No." := 0;
                SendItems."Item No." := "Item No.";
                SendItems."Inserted By" := USERID;
                SendItems."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
                IF ExternalP AND (ItemG.SkuID <> '') THEN
                  SendItems.Type := SendItems.Type::Update
                ELSE
                  SendItems.Type := TypeP;
                SendItems.INSERT(TRUE);
              END;
            END;
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN
        SendItems.RESET;
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
        SendItems.SETFILTER(Type,'<>%1',TypeP);
        SendItems.SETRANGE("Process Status",SendItems."Process Status"::" ");
        IF NOT SendItems.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
          SendItems.DELETEALL;
        END;
        IF ItemG.SkuID <> '' THEN BEGIN
          ItemCatalogEntry.RESET;
          ItemCatalogEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Item No.","Catalog Code");
          ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
          ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Catalog Code",'WEBSITE');
          IF NOT ItemCatalogEntry.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            SendItems.RESET;
            SendItems.INIT;
            SendItems."Entry No." := 0;
            SendItems."Item No." := "Item No.";
            SendItems."Inserted By" := USERID;
            SendItems."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
            SendItems.Type := TypeP;
            SendItems.INSERT(TRUE);
          END;
        END;
      END;
      //<<WI 09.17.18
    END;

    BEGIN
    {

                    MESSAGE('You did not select Update on Table, so process is canceled!');
                    EXIT;
                  END;
                  IF IsExcel THEN BEGIN
                    ExcelBuf.DELETEALL;
                    ReadExcelSheet;
                    GetLastRowandColumn;
                    TR := TotalRows;
                  END;
                  IF UpdateOnTable = UpdateOnTable::"Taxonomy Item Data" THEN BEGIN
                    InsertTaxonomyData;
                  END ELSE IF UpdateOnTable = UpdateOnTable::InsertSendItemsToWebsite THEN BEGIN
                    InsertSendItemsToWebsite;
                  END ELSE IF UpdateOnTable = UpdateOnTable::UpdateRecordsInSendItemsToWebsite THEN BEGIN
                    UpdateRecordsInSendItemsToWebsite;
                  END ELSE IF UpdateOnTable = UpdateOnTable::"Update Posting No. Into Order From Excel" THEN BEGIN
                    UpdatePostingNoIntoOrdersFromExcel
                  END ELSE IF UpdateOnTable = UpdateOnTable::"Update Posting No. Into Order" THEN BEGIN
                    UpdatePostingNoIntoOrder;
                  END ELSE IF UpdateOnTable = UpdateOnTable::Ortronics THEN BEGIN
                    InsertData;
                    MESSAGE(FORMAT(ItemsCount));
                    MESSAGE(OrtronicsItems);
                  END;
                  //MESSAGE('Process Completed!\%1 records were not Updated.',NotUpdatedG);
                  //<<HGR 07.26.18
                END;

  }

    PROCEDURE GetLastRowandColumn@1000000015();
    BEGIN
      ExcelBuf.SETRANGE("Row No.",1);
       TotalColumns := ExcelBuf.COUNT;

      ExcelBuf.RESET;
        IF ExcelBuf.FINDLAST THEN
          TotalRows := ExcelBuf."Row No.";
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetValueAtCell@1000000027(RowNo@1000000000 : Integer;ColNo@1000000001 : Integer) : Text[250];

    PROCEDURE InsertData@1000000008();
    BEGIN
      RowNo := 2;
      LineNo := 0;
       Window.OPEN(
                  Text005 +
                  '@1@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@\');
                Window.UPDATE(1,0);

      {
      REPEAT
        CLEAR(ItemNoG);
        ItemNoG := GetValueAtCell(RowNo,1);
        ItemG.RESET;
        IF NOT ItemG.GET(ItemNoG) THEN BEGIN

          IF GetValueAtCell(RowNo,1) <> '' THEN
            OldItemsDataG."Item No." := GetValueAtCell(RowNo,1);
          IF GetValueAtCell(RowNo,2) <> '' THEN
            OldItemsDataG.Description := GetValueAtCell(RowNo,2)
          ELSE
            OldItemsDataG.Description := '';
          IF UPPERCASE(GetValueAtCell(RowNo,3)) = 'YES' THEN
            OldItemsDataG."Catalog Item" := TRUE
          ELSE IF UPPERCASE(GetValueAtCell(RowNo,3)) = 'NO' THEN
            OldItemsDataG."Catalog Item" := FALSE;
          IF GetValueAtCell(RowNo,4) <> '' THEN
            OldItemsDataG."Item UPC/EAN Number" := GetValueAtCell(RowNo,4)
          ELSE
            OldItemsDataG."Item UPC/EAN Number" := '';
          OldItemsDataG.INSERT;
         END;
        Window.UPDATE(1,ROUND(RowNo / TR * 10000,1));
        RowNo += 1;
        LineNo += 1;
      UNTIL RowNo>TR;
      }

      REPEAT
        CLEAR(Ortronicspartno);
        Ortronicspartno := GetValueAtCell(RowNo,1);
        PrivateLabelsG.RESET;
        PrivateLabelsG.SETRANGE(Type,PrivateLabelsG.Type::Ortronics);
        PrivateLabelsG.SETRANGE("Ortronics Part No.",Ortronicspartno);
        IF PrivateLabelsG.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
          REPEAT
            PrivateLabelsG."Part Description1" := GetValueAtCell(RowNo,3);
            IF GetValueAtCell(RowNo,7) = 'N' THEN
              PrivateLabelsG."UL Mark" := FALSE
            ELSE IF GetValueAtCell(RowNo,7) = 'Y' THEN
              PrivateLabelsG."UL Mark" := TRUE;
              ItemsCount := ItemsCount + 1;

             PrivateLabelsG.MODIFY;
          UNTIL PrivateLabelsG.NEXT = 0;
        END ELSE
          OrtronicsItems := OrtronicsItems + Ortronicspartno;

        Window.UPDATE(1,ROUND(RowNo / TR * 10000,1));
        RowNo += 1;
        LineNo += 1;
      UNTIL RowNo>TR;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SelectSheetsName1@1000000002(FileName@1000000000 : Text) : Text;
    VAR
      selection@1000000009 : Integer;
      SheetNames@1000000013 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=2.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Collections.ArrayList";
      SheetNameLocal@1000000012 : Text[250];
      i@1000000011 : Integer;
      EndOfLoop@1000000014 : Integer;
      SheetsList@1000000015 : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      //CLEAR(XlApp);
      IF ISNULL(XlApp) THEN
        XlApp := XlApp.ApplicationClass;
      XlApp.Visible(FALSE);// FALSE if you don't want to show.
      XlWrkBk := XlApp.Workbooks.Add(FileName);
      XlWrkBk := XlApp.ActiveWorkbook;

        i := 1;
        EndOfLoop := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Count;

        WHILE i <= EndOfLoop DO BEGIN
          XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(i);
          SheetNameLocal := XlWrkSht.Name;
          IF (SheetNameLocal <> '') AND (STRLEN(SheetsList) + STRLEN(SheetNameLocal) < 250) THEN
            SheetsList := SheetsList + SheetNameLocal+ ','
          ELSE
            i := EndOfLoop;
          i := i + 1;
        END;

      selection := STRMENU(SheetsList,1);
      //---->>>
      XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(selection);
      SelectedSheetName := XlWrkSht.Name;
      XlWrkSht := XlWrkBk.Worksheets.Item(SelectedSheetName);
      //---->>>
      IF selection <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        //SelectedSheetName := SELECTSTR(selection,SheetsList);
        EXIT(SelectedSheetName);
      END ELSE
        EXIT('');
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateRecordsInSendItemsToWebsite@1000000003();
    VAR
      ItemCatalogEntry@1000000004 : Record 50081;
      SendItemstoWebsite@1000000001 : Record 50104;
      SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog@1000000005 : Record 50055;
      ItemNoL@1000000000 : Code[20];
      CountL@1000000002 : Integer;
      Totalrecords@1000000003 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      //>>HGR 08.16.18
      {
      ItemCatalogEntry.RESET;
      ItemCatalogEntry.SETRANGE("Catalog Code",'WEBSITE');
      IF ItemCatalogEntry.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        Totalrecords := ItemCatalogEntry.COUNT;
        Window.OPEN(Text008 + '@1@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@\');
        REPEAT
          SendItemstoWebsite.RESET;
          SendItemstoWebsite.SETRANGE("Item No.", ItemCatalogEntry."Item No.");
          IF SendItemstoWebsite.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              SendItemstoWebsite.Type := SendItemstoWebsite.Type::Update;
              SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status" := SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status"::" ";
              SendItemstoWebsite.MODIFY;
              Window.UPDATE(1,ROUND(CountL / Totalrecords * 10000,1));
              CountL += 1;
            UNTIL SendItemstoWebsite.NEXT = 0;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            SendItemstoWebsite.INIT;
            SendItemstoWebsite."Entry No." := 0;
            SendItemstoWebsite."Item No." := ItemCatalogEntry."Item No.";
            SendItemstoWebsite."Inserted By" := USERID;
            SendItemstoWebsite."Inserted DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
            SendItemstoWebsite.Type := SendItemstoWebsite.Type::Create;
            SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status" := SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status"::" ";
            SendItemstoWebsite.INSERT;
            Window.UPDATE(1,ROUND(CountL / Totalrecords * 10000,1));
            CountL += 1;
          END;
        UNTIL ItemCatalogEntry.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      }

      {
      WITH SendItemstoWebsite DO BEGIN
        //SETRANGE("Process Status","Process Status"::Failed);
      //  SETRANGE("Processed DateTime",CREATEDATETIME(100218D,0T),CREATEDATETIME(100218D,235900T));
        Totalrecords := COUNT;
        FINDSET;
        Window.OPEN(Text008 + '@1@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@\');
        REPEAT
          Type := Type::Update;
          "Process Status" := "Process Status"::" ";
          //SendItemstoWebsite."Processed DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
          MODIFY;

          SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.RESET;
          SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.SETRANGE("Send Items Entry No.","Entry No.");
          SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
          SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.DELETEALL;
          Window.UPDATE(1,ROUND(CountL / Totalrecords * 10000,1));
          CountL += 1;
        UNTIL NEXT = 0;
      END;
      MESSAGE('%1 of %2 records have modified!',CountL,Totalrecords);
      //<<HGR 08.16.18
      }
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdatePostingNoIntoOrder@1000000005();

      CountL@1000000002 : Integer;
      TotalCountL@1000000000 : Integer;
      SalesHeaderL@1000000003 : Record 36;
      UpdatePostingNoinOrderL@1000000004 : Record 50195;
    BEGIN
      //>>HGR 09.04.18

      UpdatePostingNoinOrderL.RESET;

        TotalCountL := UpdatePostingNoinOrderL.COUNTAPPROX;
        Window.OPEN(Text008 + '@1@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@\');

            SalesHeaderL.MODIFY;
            Window.UPDATE(1,ROUND(CountL / TotalCountL * 10000,1));
            CountL += 1;
          END ELSE MESSAGE('Not updated%1',UpdatePostingNoinOrderL);//NotUpdatedG += 1;
        UNTIL UpdatePostingNoinOrderL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      }
      //<<HGR 09.04.18
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddElement@1(VAR XMLNode@1001 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode";NodeName@1002 : Text;NodeText@1003 : Text;NameSpace@1004 : Text;VAR CreatedXMLNode@1005 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode") : Integer;
    VAR
      NewChildNode@1006 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode";
    BEGIN
      NewChildNode := XMLNode.OwnerDocument.CreateNode('element',NodeName,NameSpace);
      EXIT(AddElementToNode(XMLNode,NewChildNode,NodeText,CreatedXMLNode));
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddRootElement@21(VAR XMLDoc@1000 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlDocument";NodeName@1002 : Text;VAR CreatedXMLNode@1005 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode");
    BEGIN

      XMLDoc.AppendChild(CreatedXMLNode);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AddElementToNode@10(VAR XMLNode@1002 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode";VAR NewChildNode@1000 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode";NodeText@1001 : Text;VAR CreatedXMLNode@1003 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode") ExitStatus : Integer;
    BEGIN
      IF ISNULL(NewChildNode) THEN BEGIN
        ExitStatus := 50;
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF NodeText <> '' THEN
        NewChildNode.InnerText := NodeText;

      XMLNode.AppendChild(NewChildNode);
      CreatedXMLNode := NewChildNode;

      ExitStatus := 0;
    END;

    END;

    PROCEDURE FindNode@3(XMLRootNode@1000 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode";NodePath@1001 : Text;VAR FoundXMLNode@1002 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode") : Boolean;

    PROCEDURE AddNamespaces@19(VAR XmlNamespaceManager@1000 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNamespaceManager";XmlDocument@1005 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlDocument");

      XmlAttributeCollection := XmlDocument.DocumentElement.Attributes;

        XmlNamespaceManager.AddNamespace('',XmlDocument.DocumentElement.NamespaceURI);

      FOREACH XmlAttribute IN XmlAttributeCollection DO
        IF STRPOS(XmlAttribute.Name,'xmlns:') = 1 THEN
          XmlNamespaceManager.AddNamespace(DELSTR(XmlAttribute.Name,1,6),XmlAttribute.Value);
    END;

        IF XmlDocumentTypeOld.Name <> '' THEN
          DoctypeParams[1] := XmlDocumentTypeOld.Name;
        IF XmlDocumentTypeOld.PublicId <> '' THEN
          DoctypeParams[2] := XmlDocumentTypeOld.PublicId;
        IF XmlDocumentTypeOld.SystemId <> '' THEN
          DoctypeParams[3] := XmlDocumentTypeOld.SystemId;
        IF XmlDocumentTypeOld.InternalSubset <> '' THEN
          DoctypeParams[4] := XmlDocumentTypeOld.InternalSubset;
        XmlDocumentTypeNew := XmlDocument.CreateDocumentType(DoctypeParams[1],DoctypeParams[2],DoctypeParams[3],DoctypeParams[4]);
        XmlDocument.ReplaceChild(XmlDocumentTypeNew,XmlDocumentTypeOld);
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE LoadXmlDocFromText@31(XmlText@1004 : Text;VAR XmlDocument@1003 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlDocument";XmlReaderSettings@1005 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlReaderSettings");

      StringReader.Close;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ClearUTF8BOMSymbols@29(VAR XmlText@1000 : Text);
    VAR
      UTF8Encoding@1001 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Text.UTF8Encoding";

    END;

    PROCEDURE GetRelativePath@27(NodePath@1000 : Text;BasePath@1001 : Text) result : Text;
    VAR
      RegEx@1004 : DotNet "'System, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Text.RegularExpressions.Regex";
      BaseParts@1003 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Array";
      NodeParts@1005 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Array";
      commonCount@1006 : Integer;
      part@1007 : Integer;
      Done@1008 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF NodePath = '' THEN
        ERROR(NodePathErr);

      IF BasePath = '' THEN
        ERROR(BasePathErr);

      IF LOWERCASE(NodePath) = LOWERCASE(BasePath) THEN
        EXIT('.');

      NodeParts := RegEx.Split(NodePath,SeparatorTxt);
      BaseParts := RegEx.Split(BasePath,SeparatorTxt);

      // Cut off the common path parts
      WHILE (commonCount < NodeParts.Length) AND (commonCount < BaseParts.Length) AND NOT Done DO BEGIN
        Done := LOWERCASE(NodeParts.GetValue(commonCount)) <> LOWERCASE(BaseParts.GetValue(commonCount));
        IF NOT Done THEN
          commonCount += 1
      END;

      // Add .. for the way up from Base
      FOR part := commonCount TO BaseParts.Length - 1 DO
        result += SeparatorTxt + DotDotTxt;

      // Append the remaining part of the path
      FOR part := commonCount TO NodeParts.Length - 1 DO
        result += SeparatorTxt + FORMAT(NodeParts.GetValue(part));

      // Cut off leading separator
      result := COPYSTR(result,2);
    END;

    END;

    VAR
      StringReader@1001 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.IO.StringReader";
      XmlTextReader@1000 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlTextReader";
    BEGIN
      XmlDocument := XmlDocument.XmlDocument;

      IF XmlText = '' THEN
        EXIT;

      StringReader := StringReader.StringReader(XmlText);

      XmlDocument.Load(XmlTextReader);
      XmlTextReader.Close;
      StringReader.Close;
    END;

    PROCEDURE XMLToJSon@1000000001(tempblobp@1000000000 : Record 99008535);
    BEGIN
      tempblobp.Blob.CREATEINSTREAM(InStreamG2);
      XmlDocument := XmlDocument.XmlDocument;
      XmlDocument.Load(InStreamG2);
      ReqText := JSONConverter.SerializeXmlNode(XmlDocument.DocumentElement,JSONFormatting.Indented,FALSE);
      tempblobp.INIT;
      tempblobp.Blob.CREATEOUTSTREAM(OutstreamG2,TEXTENCODING::UTF8);
      OutstreamG2.WRITETEXT(ReqText);
    END;

    PROCEDURE JSONTextToXMLText@34(Json@1001 : Text;DocumentElementName@1000 : Text) Xml : Text;
    BEGIN
      XmlDocument := JSONConverter.DeserializeXmlNode(Json,DocumentElementName);
      Xml := XmlDocument.OuterXml;
    END;

    PROCEDURE ReadFromText@2(JSONText@1000 : Text) ErrorDetails : Text;
    VAR
      JSONTextReader@1003 : DotNet "'Newtonsoft.Json'.Newtonsoft.Json.JsonTextReader";
      StringReader@1005 : DotNet "'mscorlib, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.IO.StringReader";
      TokenType@1007 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      JSONTextReader := JSONTextReader.JsonTextReader(StringReader.StringReader(JSONText));
      IF JSONTextReader.Read THEN
        REPEAT
          IF NOT ISNULL(JSONTextReader.Value) THEN BEGIN
            IF (FORMAT(JSONTextReader.TokenType) = 'PropertyName') AND (FORMAT(JSONTextReader.Value) = 'detail') THEN
              IsErrorValue := TRUE;
            IF (IsErrorValue) AND (FORMAT(JSONTextReader.TokenType) = 'String') THEN BEGIN
              CLEAR(IsErrorValue);

            SendItemstoWebsite.RESET;

            IF SendItemstoWebsite.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
              REPEAT
                CLEARLASTERROR;
                IF NOT WebsiteIntegrationMgt.RUN(SendItemstoWebsite) THEN BEGIN
                  SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.INIT;
                  SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Entry No." := 0;
                  SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Item No." := SendItemstoWebsite."Item No.";
                  SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Send Items Entry No." := SendItemstoWebsite."Entry No.";
                  SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.Type := SendItemstoWebsite.Type;
                  SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Error Description" := COPYSTR(GETLASTERRORTEXT,1,250);
                  SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Error Log DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
                  SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.INSERT(TRUE);
                  SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status" := SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status"::Failed;
                  SendItemstoWebsite."Processed DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
                  SendItemstoWebsite.MODIFY(TRUE);
                  COMMIT;
                END;
              UNTIL SendItemstoWebsite.NEXT = 0;
            END;

            SendEmail;
          END;

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      WebsiteIntegrationMgt@1000000000 : Codeunit 50023;
      SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog@1000000001 : Record 50055;
      SendItemstoWebsite@1000000002 : Record 50104;
      ErrorTextG@1000000003 : Text;
      HasMail@1000000004 : Boolean;
      Subject@1000000008 : Text[260];
      SMTPMailSetup@1000000006 : Record 409;
      Mail@1000000005 : DotNet "'Microsoft.Dynamics.Nav.SMTP, Version=9.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=31bf3856ad364e35'.Microsoft.Dynamics.Nav.SMTP.SmtpMessage";

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SendEmail@1000000003();
    BEGIN
      SendItemstoWebsite.RESET;
      SendItemstoWebsite.SETRANGE("Process Status", SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status"::Failed);
      IF SendItemstoWebsite.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        ErrorTextG := '';
        SMTPMailSetup.GET;
        SMTPMailSetup.TESTFIELD("SMTP Server");
        IF NOT ISNULL(Mail) THEN BEGIN
          Mail.Dispose;
          CLEAR(Mail);
        END;
        Mail := Mail.SmtpMessage;
        Subject := 'Regarding Website Integration!';
        Mail.Body(('<head>'));
        Mail.AppendBody('<style>table,th,td{border:1px solid black;}</style>');
        Mail.AppendBody('</head>');
        Mail.AppendBody('<body>');
        Mail.AppendBody('Hello All,<br><br>');
        Mail.AppendBody('Below products are not updated into website.<br><br>');
        Mail.AppendBody('<Table align ="left" style="width:500px">');
        Mail.AppendBody('<TR>');
          Mail.AppendBody('<TD><B>Item No.</B></TD>');
          Mail.AppendBody('<TD><B>Type</B></TD>');
          Mail.AppendBody('<TD><B>Error Message</B></TD>');
        Mail.AppendBody('</TR>');
        REPEAT
          SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.RESET;
          SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.SETRANGE("Send Items Entry No.",SendItemstoWebsite."Entry No.");
          SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.SETRANGE("Item No.",SendItemstoWebsite."Item No.");
          SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.SETRANGE(Type,SendItemstoWebsite.Type);
          IF SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            REPEAT
              Mail.AppendBody('<TR>');
                Mail.AppendBody('<TD>'+SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Item No." +'</TD>');
                Mail.AppendBody('<TD>'+FORMAT(SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.Type) +'</TD>');
                Mail.AppendBody('<TD>'+SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Error Description" +'</TD>');
              Mail.AppendBody('</TR>');
            UNTIL SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.NEXT = 0;
          END;
        UNTIL SendItemstoWebsite.NEXT = 0;
        Mail.AppendBody('</Table>');
        Mail.AppendBody('<br><br><br><br><br><br>');
        Mail.AppendBody('Thank You<br>');
        Mail.AppendBody('Harger CC Team<br>');
        Mail.AppendBody('<hr>');
        Mail.AppendBody('PLEASE DO NOT REPLY TO THIS E-MAIL. This e-mail is generated automatically and is not monitored for responses.');
        Mail.AppendBody('</body>');
        Mail.FromName := 'NAVadmin';
        Mail.FromAddress := SMTPMailSetup."User ID";
        Mail."To" := SMTPMailSetup."Job Queue Failure Email";
        Mail.Bcc := SMTPMailSetup."User ID";
        Mail.Subject := Subject;
        Mail.HtmlFormatted := TRUE;
        ErrorTextG := Mail.Send(
                                SMTPMailSetup."SMTP Server",
                                SMTPMailSetup."SMTP Server Port",
                                SMTPMailSetup.Authentication <> SMTPMailSetup.Authentication::Anonymous,
                                SMTPMailSetup."User ID",
                                SMTPMailSetup.Password,
                                SMTPMailSetup."Secure Connection"
                                );

        Mail.Dispose;
        CLEAR(Mail);
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Harger Customizations   (Development by Sbinesh Under VLC Solutions LLC.)                              |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                      |
      ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
        HGR         03.29.18  Added new object for Calling web site integration.
    }
    END.

    PROCEDURE InitializeXMLBufferFrom@15(VAR XMLBuffer@1002 : Record 50097;StreamOrServerFile@1001 : Variant);

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateXMLReaderFrom@7(StreamOrServerFile@1000 : Variant);
    BEGIN
      CASE TRUE OF
        StreamOrServerFile.ISTEXT:
          CreateXMLReaderFromPath(StreamOrServerFile);
        StreamOrServerFile.ISINSTREAM:
          CreateXMLReaderFromInStream(StreamOrServerFile);
        StreamOrServerFile.ISOUTSTREAM:
          CreateXMLReaderFromOutStream(StreamOrServerFile);
        ELSE
          ERROR(UnsupportedInputTypeErr);
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateXMLReaderFromPath@4(Path@1000 : Text);
    BEGIN
      XmlReader := XmlReader.Create(Path,XmlReaderSettings);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateXMLReaderFromInStream@6(InStream@1000 : InStream);
    BEGIN
      XmlReader := XmlReader.Create(InStream,XmlReaderSettings);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateXMLReaderFromOutStream@24(OutStream@1000 : OutStream);
    BEGIN
      XmlReader := XmlReader.Create(OutStream,XmlReaderSettings);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CreateXmlReaderFromXmlText@12(XmlText@1000 : Text);
    BEGIN
      StringReader := StringReader.StringReader(XmlText);
      XmlReader := XmlReader.Create(StringReader);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InitializeXMLReaderSettings@5();
    BEGIN
      XmlUrlResolver := XmlUrlResolver.XmlUrlResolver;
      XmlUrlResolver.Credentials := NetCredentialCache.DefaultNetworkCredentials;

      XmlReaderSettings := XmlReaderSettings.XmlReaderSettings;
      XmlReaderSettings.DtdProcessing := XmlDtdProcessing.Ignore;
      XmlReaderSettings.XmlResolver := XmlUrlResolver;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ParseXML@14(VAR XMLBuffer@1001 : Record 50097);
    VAR
      ParentXMLBuffer@1000 : Record 50097;
    BEGIN
      IF XMLBuffer.FINDLAST THEN ;

      ParentXMLBuffer.INIT;
      IF XmlReader.Read THEN
        ParseXMLIteratively(XMLBuffer,ParentXMLBuffer);
      XmlReader.Close;
      XMLBuffer.RESET;
      XMLBuffer.SETRANGE("Import ID",XMLBuffer."Import ID");
      XMLBuffer.FINDFIRST;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ParseXMLIteratively@13(VAR XMLBuffer@1001 : Record 50097;ParentXMLBuffer@1000 : Record 50097);
    VAR
      LastInsertedXMLBufferElement@1003 : Record 50097;
      ElementNumber@1002 : Integer;
      Depth@1004 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      Depth := XmlReader.Depth;
      REPEAT
        IF IsParentElement(Depth) THEN
          EXIT;
        ParseCurrentXmlNode(XMLBuffer,ParentXMLBuffer,LastInsertedXMLBufferElement,ElementNumber,Depth);
      UNTIL NOT XmlReader.Read;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ParseCurrentXmlNode@16(VAR XMLBuffer@1001 : Record 50097;ParentXMLBuffer@1000 : Record 50097;VAR LastInsertedXMLBufferElement@1003 : Record 50097;VAR ElementNumber@1002 : Integer;Depth@1004 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      IF IsParentElement(Depth) THEN
        EXIT;
      IF IsChildElement(Depth) THEN BEGIN
        ParseXMLIteratively(XMLBuffer,LastInsertedXMLBufferElement);
        ParseCurrentXmlNode(XMLBuffer,ParentXMLBuffer,LastInsertedXMLBufferElement,ElementNumber,Depth);
      END ELSE
        ReadAndInsertXmlElement(XMLBuffer,ParentXMLBuffer,ElementNumber,LastInsertedXMLBufferElement);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE IsChildElement@10(CurrentDepth@1000 : Integer) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(XmlReader.Depth > CurrentDepth)
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE IsParentElement@20(CurrentDepth@1000 : Integer) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(XmlReader.Depth < CurrentDepth)
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ReadAndInsertXmlElement@19(VAR XMLBuffer@1001 : Record 50097;ParentXMLBuffer@1000 : Record 50097;VAR ElementNumber@1002 : Integer;VAR InsertedXMLBufferElement@1003 : Record 50097);
    VAR
      TempXMLBuffer@1004 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;
    BEGIN
      XmlNodeType := XmlReader.NodeType;
      IF XmlNodeType.Equals(XmlNodeType.Element) THEN BEGIN
        ElementNumber += 1;
        ProcessXmlElement(XMLBuffer,ParentXMLBuffer,ElementNumber,InsertedXMLBufferElement)
      END ELSE
        IF XmlNodeType.Equals(XmlNodeType.Text) THEN BEGIN
          IF XMLBuffer.ISTEMPORARY THEN BEGIN
            TempXMLBuffer.COPY(XMLBuffer,TRUE);
            TempXMLBuffer := ParentXMLBuffer;
            AddXmlTextNodeIntoParentXMLBuffer(TempXMLBuffer);
          END ELSE
            AddXmlTextNodeIntoParentXMLBuffer(ParentXMLBuffer);
        END ELSE
          IF XmlNodeType.Equals(XmlNodeType.XmlDeclaration) OR
             XmlNodeType.Equals(XmlNodeType.ProcessingInstruction) OR
             XmlNodeType.Equals(XmlNodeType.Comment)
          THEN
            ;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ProcessXmlElement@8(VAR XMLBuffer@1003 : Record 50097;ParentXMLBuffer@1000 : Record 50097;ElementNumber@1001 : Integer;VAR InsertedXMLBufferElement@1002 : Record 50097);
    VAR
      AttributeNumber@1004 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      InsertXmlElement(XMLBuffer,ParentXMLBuffer,ElementNumber);
      InsertedXMLBufferElement := XMLBuffer;

      IF XmlReader.MoveToFirstAttribute THEN
        REPEAT
          AttributeNumber += 1;
          InsertXmlAttribute(XMLBuffer,InsertedXMLBufferElement,AttributeNumber);
        UNTIL NOT XmlReader.MoveToNextAttribute;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InsertXmlElement@17(VAR XMLBuffer@1002 : Record 50097;ParentXMLBuffer@1001 : Record 50097;ElementNumber@1000 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      WITH XMLBuffer DO BEGIN
        IF OnlyGenerateStructure THEN BEGIN
          RESET;
          SETRANGE("Parent Entry No.",ParentXMLBuffer."Entry No.");
          SETRANGE(Type,Type::Element);
          SETRANGE(Name,XmlReader.Name);
          IF FINDFIRST THEN
            EXIT;
        END;

        InsertElement(XMLBuffer,ParentXMLBuffer,ElementNumber,XmlReader.Depth + 1,XmlReader.Name,'');
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE InsertXmlAttribute@18(VAR XMLBuffer@1001 : Record 50097;ParentXMLBuffer@1000 : Record 50097;AttributeNumber@1002 : Integer);
    BEGIN
      WITH XMLBuffer DO BEGIN
        IF OnlyGenerateStructure THEN BEGIN
          RESET;
          SETRANGE("Parent Entry No.",ParentXMLBuffer."Entry No.");
          SETRANGE(Type,Type::Attribute);
          SETRANGE(Name,XmlReader.Name);
          IF FINDFIRST THEN
            EXIT;
        END;

        InsertAttribute(XMLBuffer,ParentXMLBuffer,AttributeNumber,XmlReader.Depth + 1,XmlReader.Name,XmlReader.Value);
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE GetType@2(Value@1000 : Text) : Integer;
    VAR
      DummyXMLBuffer@1001 : Record 50097;
      Decimal@1003 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      IF Value = '' THEN
        EXIT(DummyXMLBuffer."Data Type"::Text);

      IF EVALUATE(Decimal,Value) THEN
        EXIT(DummyXMLBuffer."Data Type"::Decimal);

      EXIT(DummyXMLBuffer."Data Type"::Text)
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE AddXmlTextNodeIntoParentXMLBuffer@11(VAR XMLBuffer@1000 : Record 50097);
    BEGIN
      IF XMLBuffer.Value <> '' THEN
        EXIT;

      XMLBuffer.VALIDATE(Value,COPYSTR(XmlReader.Value,1,MAXSTRLEN(XMLBuffer.Value)));
      XMLBuffer.VALIDATE("Data Type",GetType(XMLBuffer.Value));
      XMLBuffer.MODIFY;
    END;

    [TryFunction]
    PROCEDURE InsertAttribute@22(VAR XMLBuffer@1000 : Record 50097;ParentXMLBuffer@1005 : Record 50097;NodeNumber@1001 : Integer;NodeDepth@1004 : Integer;AttributeName@1007 : Text[250];AttributeValue@1008 : Text[250]);
    BEGIN
      WITH XMLBuffer DO BEGIN
        RESET;
        IF FINDLAST THEN ;
        INIT;
        "Entry No." += 1;
        "Parent Entry No." := ParentXMLBuffer."Entry No.";
        Path := COPYSTR(ParentXMLBuffer.Path + '/@' + AttributeName,1,MAXSTRLEN(Path));
        "Node Number" := NodeNumber;
        Depth := NodeDepth;
        Name := AttributeName;
        Value := AttributeValue;
        "Data Type" := GetType(Value);
        Type := Type::Attribute;
        "Import ID" := ParentXMLBuffer."Import ID";

        INSERT;
      END;
    END;

    [TryFunction]
    PROCEDURE InsertElement@21(VAR XMLBuffer@1010 : Record 50097;ParentXMLBuffer@1009 : Record 50097;ElementNumber@1003 : Integer;ElementDepth@1006 : Integer;ElementNameAndNamespace@1008 : Text[250];ElementValue@1007 : Text[250]);
    VAR
      ElementName@1000 : Text[250];
      ElementNamespace@1005 : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      SplitXmlElementName(ElementNameAndNamespace,ElementName,ElementNamespace);

      IF ISNULLGUID(ParentXMLBuffer."Import ID") THEN
        ParentXMLBuffer."Import ID" := CREATEGUID;

      WITH XMLBuffer DO BEGIN
        RESET;
        IF FINDLAST THEN ;
        INIT;
        "Entry No." += 1;
        "Parent Entry No." := ParentXMLBuffer."Entry No.";
        Path := COPYSTR(STRSUBSTNO('%1/%2',ParentXMLBuffer.Path,ElementNameAndNamespace),1,MAXSTRLEN(Path));
        "Node Number" := ElementNumber;
        Depth := ElementDepth;
        Name := ElementName;
        Value := ElementValue;
        Type := Type::Element;
        Namespace := ElementNamespace;
        "Import ID" := ParentXMLBuffer."Import ID";

        INSERT;
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SplitXmlElementName@46(RawXmlElementName@1000 : Text[250];VAR ElementName@1001 : Text[250];VAR ElementNamespace@1002 : Text[250]);
    VAR
      ColonPosition@1003 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      ColonPosition := STRPOS(RawXmlElementName,':');
      IF ColonPosition <> 0 THEN BEGIN
        ElementNamespace := COPYSTR(RawXmlElementName,1,ColonPosition - 1);
        ElementName := COPYSTR(RawXmlElementName,ColonPosition + 1);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        ElementName := RawXmlElementName;
        ElementNamespace := '';
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Harger Customizations   (Development by Sbinesh Under VLC Solutions LLC.)                              |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                      |
      ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
        HGR         03.29.18  Added new object for XML functionality.
    }
    END.
  }

OBJECT Codeunit 50058 XML Buffer Reader V2
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=03/29/18;
    Time=[ 1:00:00 AM];

  }

  {
    OnRun=BEGIN
          END;

  }
  CODE
  {
    VAR
      DefaultNamespace@1000 : Text;

    [TryFunction]
    PROCEDURE SaveToFile@7(FilePath@1000 : Text;VAR XMLBuffer@1001 : Record 50097);
    VAR
      TempXMLBuffer@1004 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;
      TempAttributeXMLBuffer@1003 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;
      XMLDOMManagement@1005 : Codeunit 6224;
      XmlDocument@1007 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlDocument";
      RootElement@1006 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode";
      Header@1002 : Text;
    BEGIN
      TempXMLBuffer.CopyImportFrom(XMLBuffer);
      TempXMLBuffer := XMLBuffer;
      TempXMLBuffer.SETCURRENTKEY("Parent Entry No.",Type,"Node Number");
      Header := '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>' +
        '<' + TempXMLBuffer.GetElementName + ' ';

      DefaultNamespace := TempXMLBuffer.GetAttributeValue('xmlns');
      IF TempXMLBuffer.FindAttributes(TempAttributeXMLBuffer) THEN
        REPEAT
          Header += TempAttributeXMLBuffer.Name + '="' + TempAttributeXMLBuffer.Value + '" ';
        UNTIL TempAttributeXMLBuffer.NEXT = 0;
      Header += '/>';

      XMLDOMManagement.LoadXMLDocumentFromTextV1(Header,XmlDocument);
      RootElement := XmlDocument.DocumentElement;

      SaveChildElements(TempXMLBuffer,RootElement,XmlDocument);

      XmlDocument.Save(FilePath);
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SaveChildElements@33(VAR TempParentElementXMLBuffer@1000 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;XMLCurrElement@1002 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode";XmlDocument@1003 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlDocument");
    VAR
      TempElementXMLBuffer@1001 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;
      ChildElement@1005 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode";
      Namespace@1006 : Text;
    BEGIN
      IF TempParentElementXMLBuffer.FindChildElements(TempElementXMLBuffer) THEN
        REPEAT
          IF TempElementXMLBuffer.Namespace = '' THEN
            Namespace := DefaultNamespace
          ELSE
            Namespace := TempElementXMLBuffer.Namespace;
          ChildElement := XmlDocument.CreateNode('element',TempElementXMLBuffer.GetElementName,Namespace);
          IF TempElementXMLBuffer.Value <> '' THEN
            ChildElement.InnerText := TempElementXMLBuffer.Value;
          XMLCurrElement.AppendChild(ChildElement);
          SaveAttributes(TempElementXMLBuffer,ChildElement,XmlDocument);
          SaveChildElements(TempElementXMLBuffer,ChildElement,XmlDocument);
        UNTIL TempElementXMLBuffer.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE SaveAttributes@9(VAR TempParentElementXMLBuffer@1001 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;XMLCurrElement@1002 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlNode";XmlDocument@1003 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlDocument");
    VAR
      TempAttributeXMLBuffer@1000 : TEMPORARY Record 50097;
      Attribute@1005 : DotNet "'System.Xml, Version=4.0.0.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=b77a5c561934e089'.System.Xml.XmlAttribute";
    BEGIN
      IF TempParentElementXMLBuffer.FindAttributes(TempAttributeXMLBuffer) THEN
        REPEAT
          Attribute := XmlDocument.CreateAttribute(TempAttributeXMLBuffer.Name);
          Attribute.InnerText := TempAttributeXMLBuffer.Value;
          XMLCurrElement.Attributes.SetNamedItem(Attribute);
        UNTIL TempAttributeXMLBuffer.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Harger Customizations   (Development by Sbinesh Under VLC Solutions LLC.)                              |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                      |
      ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
        HGR         03.29.18  Added new object for XML functionality.
    }
    END.
  }
}

    PROCEDURE GetFilesList@1000000000(FTPAddress@1000000000 : Text;Login@1000000001 : Text;Password@1000000002 : Text) : Integer;
    BEGIN
      FTPRequest := FTPRequest.Create(FTPAddress);
      Credentials := Credentials.NetworkCredential(Login,Password);
      FTPRequest.Credentials := Credentials;
      FTPRequest.KeepAlive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.Method := 'NLST';
      FTPRequest.UsePassive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.UseBinary := TRUE;

      FTPResponse := FTPRequest.GetResponse;
      ResponseStream := FTPResponse.GetResponseStream();
      StreamReader := StreamReader.StreamReader(ResponseStream);
      FilesList := FilesList.ArrayList;
      WHILE NOT StreamReader.EndOfStream DO BEGIN
        FilesList.Add(StreamReader.ReadLine);
      END;

      StreamReader.Close;
      ResponseStream.Close;
      FTPResponse.Close;
      EXIT(FilesList.Count);
    END;

    PROCEDURE DownloadFileAnonymous@1000000001(FTPAddressFile@1000000000 : Text;DownloadToFile@1000000004 : Text);
    BEGIN
      FTPRequest := FTPRequest.Create(FTPAddressFile);
      Credentials := Credentials.NetworkCredential();
      FTPRequest.Credentials := Credentials;
      FTPRequest.KeepAlive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.Method := 'RETR';
      FTPRequest.UsePassive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.UseBinary := TRUE;

      FTPResponse := FTPRequest.GetResponse;
      ResponseStream := FTPResponse.GetResponseStream();
      SimpleStream := FileStream.Create(DownloadToFile);
      ResponseStream.CopyTo(SimpleStream);
      SimpleStream.Close;
      ResponseStream.Close;
      FTPResponse.Close;
      IF GUIALLOWED THEN
        MESSAGE('Download Successfully!');
    END;

    PROCEDURE DownloadFile@1000000003(FTPAddressFile@1000000000 : Text;DownloadToFile@1000000004 : Text;Login@1000000001 : Text;Password@1000000002 : Text;DeleteAfterDownload@1000000005 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      FTPRequest := FTPRequest.Create(FTPAddressFile);
      Credentials := Credentials.NetworkCredential(Login,Password);
      FTPRequest.Credentials := Credentials;
      FTPRequest.KeepAlive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.Method := 'RETR';
      FTPRequest.UsePassive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.UseBinary := TRUE;
      SLEEP(10000);//added
      FTPResponse := FTPRequest.GetResponse;
      ResponseStream := FTPResponse.GetResponseStream();
      SimpleStream := FileStream.Create(DownloadToFile);
      ResponseStream.CopyTo(SimpleStream);
      SimpleStream.Close;
      ResponseStream.Close;
      FTPResponse.Close;
      IF DeleteAfterDownload THEN BEGIN
        DeleteFile(FTPAddressFile,Login,Password);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeleteFile@1000000004(FTPAddressFile@1000000000 : Text;Login@1000000001 : Text;Password@1000000002 : Text) : Boolean;
    VAR
      Deleted@1000000004 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(Deleted);
      FTPRequest := FTPRequest.Create(FTPAddressFile);
      Credentials := Credentials.NetworkCredential(Login,Password);
      FTPRequest.Credentials := Credentials;
      FTPRequest.KeepAlive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.Method := 'DELE';
      FTPRequest.UsePassive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.UseBinary := TRUE;
      StatusCode := FTPResponse.StatusCode;
      FTPResponse := FTPRequest.GetResponse;
      IF FTPResponse.StatusCode.ToString() = StatusCode.FileActionOK.ToString() THEN BEGIN
        Deleted := TRUE;
      END;
      FTPResponse.Close;
      EXIT(Deleted);
    END;

    PROCEDURE UploadFile@1000000002(FileNameToUpload@1000000000 : Text;UploadToFtp@1000000004 : Text;Login@1000000001 : Text;Password@1000000002 : Text);
    BEGIN
      FTPRequest := FTPRequest.Create(UploadToFtp);
      Credentials := Credentials.NetworkCredential(Login,Password);
      FTPRequest.Credentials := Credentials;
      FTPRequest.KeepAlive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.Method := 'STOR';
      FTPRequest.UsePassive := TRUE;
      FTPRequest.UseBinary := TRUE;
      RealFileStream := FileStream.OpenRead(FileNameToUpload);
      SimpleStream := FTPRequest.GetRequestStream;
      RealFileStream.CopyTo(SimpleStream);
      SimpleStream.Close;
      RealFileStream.Close;
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetFilename@1000000005(Index@1000000000 : Integer) : Text;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(FORMAT(FilesList.Item(Index)));
    END;

    PROCEDURE DownloadFiles@1000000006(FTPAddressWithFolder@1000000002 : Text;DownloadToFolder@1000000003 : Text;FTPUserID@1000000004 : Text;FTPPassword@1000000005 : Text);
    VAR
      Counter@1000000000 : Integer;
      FilesCount@1000000001 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      FilesCount := GetFilesList(FTPAddressWithFolder,FTPUserID,FTPPassword);
      IF FilesCount > 0 THEN BEGIN
        FOR Counter := 0 TO FilesCount - 1 DO BEGIN
          DownloadFile(FTPAddressWithFolder + GetFilename(Counter),DownloadToFolder + GetFilename(Counter),FTPUserID,FTPPassword,FALSE);//TRUE TO DELETE
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE UploadFiles@1000000007(UploadFromFolder@1000000002 : Text;UploadToFTPAddressWithFolder@1000000003 : Text;FTPUserID@1000000005 : Text;FTPPassword@1000000004 : Text);
    BEGIN
      Files.RESET;
      Files.SETRANGE(Path,UploadFromFolder);
      Files.SETRANGE("Is a file",TRUE);
      IF Files.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          UploadFile(Files.Path + Files.Name,UploadToFTPAddressWithFolder + Files.Name,FTPUserID,FTPPassword);
        UNTIL Files.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Harger Customizations   (Development by Sbinesh Under VLC Solutions LLC.)                              |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
      | Job No.     Date      Description                                                                      |
      +--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
        HGR          10.11.18  Added new object for FTP Management.
    }
    END.
  }

    [TryFunction]
    PROCEDURE ExportDocument@1000000016(DocNoP@1000000002 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      DocumentL@1000000000 : Record 50066;
      OutStream@1000000005 : OutStream;
      InStream@1000000004 : InStream;
      OutputFile@1000000003 : File;
    BEGIN
      DocumentL.GET(DocNoP);
      IF DocumentL.CALCFIELDS(Content) THEN BEGIN
        IF DocumentL.Content.HASVALUE THEN BEGIN
          ExportFile := DocumentSetup."Temp Path" + DocumentL."No." + '.' + DocumentL."File Extension";
          IF EXISTS(ExportFile) THEN ERASE(ExportFile);
          OutputFile.WRITEMODE(TRUE);
          OutputFile.CREATE(ExportFile);
          OutputFile.CREATEOUTSTREAM(OutStream);
          DocumentL.Content.CREATEINSTREAM(InStream);
          IF NOT COPYSTREAM(OutStream,InStream) THEN ERROR(GETLASTERRORTEXT);
          OutputFile.CLOSE;

          IF NOT UploadFile(ExportFile) THEN
          BEGIN
            CLEARLASTERROR;
            SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.INIT;
            SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Entry No." := 0;
            SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Send Items Entry No." := SendItemstoWebsite."Entry No.";
            SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Product Type" := SendItemstoWebsite."Product Type";
            SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Item No." := SendItemstoWebsite."Item No.";
            SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.Type := SendItemstoWebsite.Type;
            IF STRLEN(GETLASTERRORTEXT) > 250 THEN
              SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Error Description" := COPYSTR(GETLASTERRORTEXT,1,250)
            ELSE
              SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Error Description" := GETLASTERRORTEXT;
            SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Error Log DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
            SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog."Response Code" := 'Error on Uploading to SFTP';
            SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.INSERT(TRUE);

            SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status" := SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status"::Failed;
            SendItemstoWebsite."Processed DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
            SendItemstoWebsite.MODIFY;
          END ELSE BEGIN
            IF EXISTS(ExportFile) THEN ERASE(ExportFile);
            SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status" := SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status"::" ";
            SendItemstoWebsite."Processed DateTime" := CURRENTDATETIME;
            SendItemstoWebsite.MODIFY;
          END;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    [TryFunction]
    LOCAL PROCEDURE UploadFile@1000000003(SourceFileP@1000000000 : Text);
    BEGIN
      GetDocumentSetup;
      WinSCPSessionOptions := WinSCPSessionOptions.SessionOptions();
      WinSCPSessionOptions.Protocol := WinSCPProtocol.Sftp;
      WinSCPSessionOptions.HostName := DocumentSetup."SFTP HostName";
      WinSCPSessionOptions.PortNumber := DocumentSetup."SFTP Port";
      WinSCPSessionOptions.UserName := DocumentSetup."SFTP User Name";
      WinSCPSessionOptions.Password := DocumentSetup."SFTP Password";
      WinSCPSessionOptions.SshHostKeyFingerprint := DocumentSetup."SFTP Host Key";

      WinSCPSesh := WinSCPSesh.Session();
      WinSCPSesh.ExecutablePath(WinSCP_Executable_Path);
      WinSCPSesh.Open(WinSCPSessionOptions);
      IF WinSCPSesh.Opened THEN BEGIN
        WinSCPTransferOptions := WinSCPTransferOptions.TransferOptions;
        WinSCPTransferOptions.TransferMode := 0;
        WinSCPTransferResumeSupport := WinSCPTransferOptions.ResumeSupport;
        WinSCPTransferResumeSupport.State(WinSCPTransferResumeSupportState.Off);

        IF WinSCPSesh.FileExists(WinSCPSesh.HomePath()+'uploads/'+FileManagement.GetFileName(SourceFileP)) THEN
          WinSCPSesh.RemoveFiles(WinSCPSesh.HomePath()+'uploads/'+FileManagement.GetFileName(SourceFileP));
        WinSCPTransferResults :=
                  WinSCPSesh.PutFiles(SourceFileP,
                                      WinSCPSesh.HomePath()+'uploads/',
                                      FALSE,
                                      WinSCPTransferOptions
                                      );
      END ELSE ERROR('Connection Failed!');

      IF WinSCPSesh.Opened THEN WinSCPSesh.Dispose();
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CountFiles@1000000006() CountL : Integer;
    BEGIN
      GetDocumentSetup;
      WinSCPSessionOptions := WinSCPSessionOptions.SessionOptions();
      WinSCPSessionOptions.Protocol := WinSCPProtocol.Sftp;
      WinSCPSessionOptions.HostName := DocumentSetup."SFTP HostName";
      WinSCPSessionOptions.PortNumber := DocumentSetup."SFTP Port";
      WinSCPSessionOptions.UserName := DocumentSetup."SFTP User Name";
      WinSCPSessionOptions.Password := DocumentSetup."SFTP Password";
      WinSCPSessionOptions.SshHostKeyFingerprint := DocumentSetup."SFTP Host Key";

      WinSCPSesh := WinSCPSesh.Session();
      WinSCPSesh.ExecutablePath(WinSCP_Executable_Path);
      WinSCPSesh.Open(WinSCPSessionOptions);
      IF WinSCPSesh.Opened THEN BEGIN
        WinSCPRemoteInfoColl := WinSCPSesh.ListDirectory(WinSCPSesh.HomePath()+'uploads/');
        WinSCPRemoteInfo := WinSCPRemoteInfoColl.Files();
        CLEAR(CountL);
        FOREACH WinSCPRemoteInfo IN WinSCPRemoteInfoColl.Files DO
          IF NOT WinSCPRemoteInfo.IsDirectory THEN
            CountL += 1;
      END ELSE ERROR('Connection Failed!');

      IF WinSCPSesh.Opened THEN WinSCPSesh.Dispose();
      EXIT(CountL);
    END;

                      CaptionML=ENU=Clear Log & Re Send;
                      Promoted=Yes;
                      PromotedIsBig=Yes;
                      Image=ClearLog;
                      PromotedCategory=Process;
                      OnAction=BEGIN
                                 SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.RESET;
                                 SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.SETRANGE(Type,Type);
                                 SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.SETRANGE("Item No.","Item No.");
                                 SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.SETRANGE("Send Items Entry No.", "Send Items Entry No.");
                                 IF SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                                   IF SendItemstoWebsite.GET("Send Items Entry No.") THEN BEGIN
                                     SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status" := SendItemstoWebsite."Process Status"::" ";
                                     SendItemstoWebsite.MODIFY;
                                   END;
                                   SendItemtoWebsiteErrorsLog.DELETEALL;
                                   CurrPage.CLOSE;
                                 END;
                               END;
                                }
    }
  }
